Geometry-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Multi-view Consistent 3D Scene Editing
Authors: Jiyuan Wang, Chunyu Lin, Lei Sun, Zhi Cao, Yuyang Yin, Lang Nie, Zhenlong Yuan, Xiangxiang Chu, Yunchao Wei, Kang Liao, Guosheng Lin
First: 2026-03-03T16:31:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:31:10+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Leveraging the priors of 2D diffusion models for 3D editing has emerged as a promising paradigm. However, maintaining multi-view consistency in edited results remains challenging, and the extreme scarcity of 3D-consistent editing paired data renders supervised fine-tuning (SFT), the most effective training strategy for editing tasks, infeasible. In this paper, we observe that, while generating multi-view consistent 3D content is highly challenging, verifying 3D consistency is tractable, naturally positioning reinforcement learning (RL) as a feasible solution. Motivated by this, we propose \textbf{RL3DEdit}, a single-pass framework driven by RL optimization with novel rewards derived from the 3D foundation model, VGGT. Specifically, we leverage VGGT's robust priors learned from massive real-world data, feed the edited images, and utilize the output confidence maps and pose estimation errors as reward signals, effectively anchoring the 2D editing priors onto a 3D-consistent manifold via RL. Extensive experiments demonstrate that RL3DEdit achieves stable multi-view consistency and outperforms state-of-the-art methods in editing quality with high efficiency. To promote the development of 3D editing, we will release the code and model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：几何引导的强化学习实现多视角一致的3D场景编辑
利用二维扩散模型先验进行三维编辑已成为前景广阔的研究范式。然而，保持编辑结果的多视角一致性仍具挑战性，且三维一致性编辑配对数据的极度稀缺使得监督微调——编辑任务中最有效的训练策略——难以实施。本文发现，虽然生成多视角一致的三维内容极具挑战性，但验证三维一致性是可实现的，这自然使强化学习成为可行解决方案。基于此，我们提出\textbf{RL3DEdit}：一种由强化学习优化的单次处理框架，其创新奖励信号源自三维基础模型VGGT。具体而言，我们利用VGGT从海量真实数据中学到的强健先验，输入编辑后的图像，并将输出的置信度图与姿态估计误差作为奖励信号，通过强化学习将二维编辑先验有效锚定在三维一致性流形上。大量实验表明，RL3DEdit能稳定实现多视角一致性，在编辑质量上以高效性超越现有先进方法。为促进三维编辑领域发展，我们将公开代码与模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of maintaining multi-view consistency in 3D scene editing using 2D diffusion priors and the infeasibility of supervised fine-tuning due to data scarcity, this paper proposes RL3DEdit, a reinforcement learning framework. The method uses novel reward signals derived from a 3D foundation model (VGGT), specifically its confidence maps and pose estimation errors, to guide the RL optimization and anchor 2D editing priors onto a 3D-consistent manifold. Experimental results show that RL3DEdit achieves stable multi-view consistency, outperforms state-of-the-art methods in editing quality, and operates efficiently.
针对利用2D扩散模型先验进行3D场景编辑时难以保持多视角一致性的挑战，以及由于配对数据稀缺导致监督微调不可行的问题，本文提出了RL3DEdit，一个基于强化学习的框架。该方法利用3D基础模型VGGT输出的置信度图和姿态估计误差作为新颖的奖励信号，通过强化学习优化将2D编辑先验锚定到3D一致流形上。实验结果表明，RL3DEdit实现了稳定的多视角一致性，在编辑质量上优于现有先进方法，且运行高效。
Proactive Guiding Strategy for Item-side Fairness in Interactive Recommendation
Authors: Chongjun Xia, Xiaoyu Shi, Hong Xie, Xianzhi Wang, yun lu, Mingsheng Shang
First: 2026-03-03T15:32:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T15:32:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Item-side fairness is crucial for ensuring the fair exposure of long-tail items in interactive recommender systems. Existing approaches promote the exposure of long-tail items by directly incorporating them into recommended results. This causes misalignment between user preferences and the recommended long-tail items, which hinders long-term user engagement and reduces the effectiveness of recommendations. We aim for a proactive fairness-guiding strategy, which actively guides user preferences toward long-tail items while preserving user satisfaction during the interactive recommendation process. To this end, we propose HRL4PFG, an interactive recommendation framework that leverages hierarchical reinforcement learning to guide user preferences toward long-tail items progressively. HRL4PFG operates through a macro-level process that generates fairness-guided targets based on multi-step feedback, and a micro-level process that fine-tunes recommendations in real time according to both these targets and evolving user preferences. Extensive experiments show that HRL4PFG improves cumulative interaction rewards and maximum user interaction length by a larger margin when compared with state-of-the-art methods in interactive recommendation environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：交互式推荐中面向项目侧公平性的主动引导策略
项目侧公平性对于确保交互式推荐系统中长尾项目的公平曝光至关重要。现有方法通过直接将长尾项目纳入推荐结果来促进其曝光，但这会导致用户偏好与推荐的长尾项目之间不匹配，从而阻碍长期用户参与度并降低推荐效果。我们提出一种主动公平引导策略，在交互推荐过程中积极引导用户偏好向长尾项目倾斜，同时保持用户满意度。为此，我们提出HRL4PFG框架，该框架利用分层强化学习逐步引导用户偏好转向长尾项目。HRL4PFG通过宏观层面（基于多步反馈生成公平引导目标）和微观层面（根据这些目标及动态用户偏好实时微调推荐）协同运作。大量实验表明，在交互推荐环境中，与前沿方法相比，HRL4PFG能更大程度提升累积交互奖励和最大用户交互长度。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of ensuring item-side fairness in interactive recommender systems, where existing methods often misalign with user preferences by directly inserting long-tail items, thereby harming user engagement. The authors propose HRL4PFG, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework that proactively guides user preferences toward long-tail items through a two-level process: a macro-level component sets fairness-guided targets using multi-step feedback, while a micro-level component fine-tunes recommendations in real time based on these targets and dynamic user preferences. Experimental results demonstrate that HRL4PFG significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods by improving cumulative interaction rewards and extending maximum user interaction length in interactive recommendation environments.
本文针对交互式推荐系统中项目侧公平性的挑战，指出现有方法直接插入长尾项目常导致与用户偏好错位，损害用户参与度。作者提出HRL4PFG，一种分层强化学习框架，通过双层过程主动引导用户偏好向长尾项目发展：宏观层面基于多步反馈生成公平性引导目标，微观层面则根据这些目标和动态用户偏好实时微调推荐。实验结果表明，在交互推荐环境中，HRL4PFG显著优于现有先进方法，提高了累积交互奖励并延长了最大用户交互长度。
RAPO: Expanding Exploration for LLM Agents via Retrieval-Augmented Policy Optimization
Authors: Siwei Zhang, Yun Xiong, Xi Chen, Zi'an Jia, Renhong Huang, Jiarong Xu, Jiawei Zhang
Venue: KDD 2026
First: 2026-03-03T15:23:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T15:23:42+00:00
Comments: Submit to KDD 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic Reinforcement Learning (Agentic RL) has shown remarkable potential in large language model-based (LLM) agents. These works can empower LLM agents to tackle complex tasks via multi-step, tool-integrated reasoning. However, an inherent limitation of existing Agentic RL methods is their reliance on a pure on-policy paradigm for exploration, restricting exploration to the agent's self-generated outputs and preventing the discovery of new reasoning perspectives for further improvement. While recent efforts incorporate auxiliary off-policy signals to enhance exploration, they typically utilize full off-policy trajectories for trajectory-level policy estimation, overlooking the necessity for the fine-grained, step-level exploratory dynamics within agentic rollout. In this paper, we revisit exploration in Agentic RL and propose Retrieval-Augmented Policy Optimization (RAPO), a novel RL framework that introduces retrieval to explicitly expand exploration during training. To achieve this, we decompose the Agentic RL training process into two phases: (i) Hybrid-policy Agentic Rollout, and (ii) Retrieval-aware Policy Optimization. Specifically, we propose a Hybrid-policy Agentic Rollout strategy, which allows the agents to continuously reason over the retrieved off-policy step-level traces. It dynamically extends the reasoning receptive field of agents, enabling broader exploration conditioned on external behaviors. Subsequently, we introduce the Retrieval-aware Policy Optimization mechanism, which calibrates the policy gradient estimation with retrieval reward and importance shaping, stabilizing training and prioritizing retrieval-illuminating exploration. Extensive experiments show that RAPO achieves an +5.0% average gain on fourteen datasets across three agentic reasoning tasks, while delivering 1.2x faster training efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RAPO：基于检索增强策略优化的LLM智能体探索扩展方法
智能体强化学习在基于大语言模型的智能体中展现出显著潜力，能通过多步骤、工具集成的推理处理复杂任务。然而，现有方法依赖纯在线策略范式进行探索，限制了智能体对自身生成输出的探索范围，难以发现新的推理视角以进一步提升性能。近期研究虽引入辅助离线策略信号增强探索，但通常采用完整轨迹进行策略估计，忽略了智能体推演过程中细粒度、步骤级探索动态的必要性。本文重新审视智能体强化学习的探索机制，提出检索增强策略优化框架，通过显式引入检索扩展训练阶段的探索范围。具体实现分为两个阶段：（1）混合策略智能体推演：设计混合策略推演策略，使智能体能持续基于检索的离线策略步骤级轨迹进行推理，动态扩展智能体的推理感知域，实现基于外部行为的广谱探索；（2）检索感知策略优化：通过检索奖励与重要性加权校准策略梯度估计，稳定训练过程并优先促进检索启发性探索。在三个智能体推理任务的十四组数据集上的实验表明，RAPO实现平均5.0%的性能提升，同时训练效率提升1.2倍。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitation of existing Agentic Reinforcement Learning methods for LLM agents, which rely on a pure on-policy paradigm for exploration, restricting agents to self-generated outputs and hindering the discovery of new reasoning perspectives. To address this, the authors propose Retrieval-Augmented Policy Optimization (RAPO), a novel RL framework that introduces retrieval to explicitly expand exploration through a two-phase process: a Hybrid-policy Agentic Rollout that allows agents to reason over retrieved off-policy step-level traces, and a Retrieval-aware Policy Optimization mechanism that calibrates policy gradient estimation with retrieval reward and importance shaping. Experimental results demonstrate that RAPO achieves an average performance gain of +5.0% across fourteen datasets in three agentic reasoning tasks while improving training efficiency by 1.2 times.
本文的动机在于现有基于大语言模型的智能体强化学习方法存在局限性，其依赖于纯策略内探索范式，将探索限制在智能体自身生成的输出中，阻碍了新推理视角的发现。为解决这一问题，作者提出了检索增强策略优化（RAPO），这是一个新颖的强化学习框架，通过引入检索来显式扩展探索，其过程分为两个阶段：混合策略智能体推演，使智能体能基于检索到的策略外步级轨迹进行推理；以及检索感知策略优化机制，通过检索奖励和重要性调整来校准策略梯度估计。实验结果表明，RAPO在三个智能体推理任务的十四个数据集上平均性能提升了5.0%，同时训练效率提高了1.2倍。
TikZilla: Scaling Text-to-TikZ with High-Quality Data and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Christian Greisinger, Steffen Eger
First: 2026-03-03T15:17:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T15:17:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to assist scientists across diverse workflows. A key challenge is generating high-quality figures from textual descriptions, often represented as TikZ programs that can be rendered as scientific images. Prior research has proposed a variety of datasets and modeling approaches for this task. However, existing datasets for Text-to-TikZ are too small and noisy to capture the complexity of TikZ, causing mismatches between text and rendered figures. Moreover, prior approaches rely solely on supervised fine-tuning (SFT), which does not expose the model to the rendered semantics of the figure, often resulting in errors such as looping, irrelevant content, and incorrect spatial relations. To address these issues, we construct DaTikZ-V4, a dataset more than four times larger and substantially higher in quality than DaTikZ-V3, enriched with LLM-generated figure descriptions. Using this dataset, we train TikZilla, a family of small open-source Qwen models (3B and 8B) with a two-stage pipeline of SFT followed by reinforcement learning (RL). For RL, we leverage an image encoder trained via inverse graphics to provide semantically faithful reward signals. Extensive human evaluations with over 1,000 judgments show that TikZilla improves by 1.5-2 points over its base models on a 5-point scale, surpasses GPT-4o by 0.5 points, and matches GPT-5 in the image-based evaluation, while operating at much smaller model sizes. Code, data, and models will be made available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TikZilla：通过高质量数据与强化学习实现文本到TikZ的规模化生成
大语言模型（LLMs）正日益广泛地应用于辅助科学家的多样化工作流程。其中，从文本描述生成高质量图表是一个关键挑战，这类描述通常以可渲染为科学图像的TikZ程序表示。先前研究已为此任务提出了多种数据集和建模方法。然而，现有的文本到TikZ数据集规模过小且噪声较多，难以捕捉TikZ的复杂性，导致文本与渲染图像之间存在不匹配。此外，现有方法仅依赖监督微调（SFT），未让模型接触图像的渲染语义，常产生循环结构、无关内容或空间关系错误等问题。为解决这些问题，我们构建了DaTikZ-V4数据集，其规模是DaTikZ-V3的四倍以上，质量显著提升，并融合了LLM生成的图像描述。基于此数据集，我们训练了TikZilla系列模型——采用3B和8B参数的小型开源Qwen模型，通过SFT后接强化学习（RL）的两阶段流程进行训练。在RL阶段，我们利用通过逆向图形训练的图像编码器提供语义保真的奖励信号。基于超1,000条判断的广泛人工评估表明，TikZilla在5分制评分中较基础模型提升1.5-2分，超越GPT-4o 0.5分，在基于图像的评估中与GPT-5表现相当，且模型规模显著更小。代码、数据与模型将公开提供。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of generating high-quality scientific figures from text descriptions using TikZ code, noting that existing datasets are too small and noisy, and supervised fine-tuning alone fails to capture rendered semantics, leading to errors. To overcome this, the authors construct DaTikZ-V4, a significantly larger and higher-quality dataset enhanced with LLM-generated descriptions, and train TikZilla models using a two-stage pipeline: supervised fine-tuning followed by reinforcement learning with reward signals from an image encoder trained via inverse graphics. Experimental results from human evaluations show that TikZilla improves over base models by 1.5-2 points on a 5-point scale, surpasses GPT-4o by 0.5 points, and matches GPT-5 in image-based evaluation, despite using smaller model sizes.
本文针对从文本描述生成高质量科学图表（使用TikZ代码）的挑战，指出现有数据集规模小、噪声多，且仅依赖监督微调无法捕捉渲染语义，导致循环、无关内容等错误。为解决这些问题，作者构建了DaTikZ-V4数据集，其规模和质量远超先前版本，并利用LLM生成描述增强数据，随后采用两阶段流程训练TikZilla模型：先进行监督微调，再通过强化学习结合基于逆向图形训练的图像编码器提供奖励信号。实验结果表明，在人类评估中，TikZilla比基础模型提升1.5-2分（5分制），超过GPT-4o 0.5分，并在基于图像的评估中与GPT-5相当，同时模型规模更小。
Reinforcement Learning with Symbolic Reward Machines
Authors: Thomas Krug, Daniel Neider
First: 2026-03-03T15:11:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T15:11:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward Machines (RMs) are an established mechanism in Reinforcement Learning (RL) to represent and learn sparse, temporally extended tasks with non-Markovian rewards. RMs rely on high-level information in the form of labels that are emitted by the environment alongside the observation. However, this concept requires manual user input for each environment and task. The user has to create a suitable labeling function that computes the labels. These limitations lead to poor applicability in widely adopted RL frameworks. We propose Symbolic Reward Machines (SRMs) together with the learning algorithms QSRM and LSRM to overcome the limitations of RMs. SRMs consume only the standard output of the environment and process the observation directly through guards that are represented by symbolic formulas. In our evaluation, our SRM methods outperform the baseline RL approaches and generate the same results as the existing RM methods. At the same time, our methods adhere to the widely used environment definition and provide interpretable representations of the task to the user.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于符号奖励机制的强化学习
奖励机制（RMs）是强化学习（RL）中一种成熟的机制，用于表示和学习具有非马尔可夫奖励的稀疏、时间扩展任务。RMs依赖于环境与观察同时发出的标签形式的高层信息。然而，这一概念需要用户为每个环境和任务手动输入，即创建合适的标签函数来计算标签。这些限制导致其在广泛采用的RL框架中适用性较差。我们提出了符号奖励机制（SRMs）及学习算法QSRM和LSRM，以克服RMs的局限性。SRMs仅消耗环境的标准输出，并通过符号公式表示的守卫直接处理观察。在我们的评估中，SRM方法优于基线RL方法，并产生与现有RM方法相同的结果。同时，我们的方法遵循广泛使用的环境定义，并向用户提供任务的可解释表示。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of Reward Machines (RMs) in Reinforcement Learning, which require manual design of labeling functions for each environment and task, hindering their broad applicability. The method introduces Symbolic Reward Machines (SRMs) with algorithms QSRM and LSRM, which process raw environment observations directly using symbolic formulas as guards, eliminating the need for pre-defined labels. The main experimental results show that the SRM methods outperform baseline RL approaches and match the performance of existing RM methods, while adhering to standard environment interfaces and providing interpretable task representations.
本研究的动机是克服强化学习中奖励机器的局限性，后者需要为每个环境和任务手动设计标签函数，阻碍了其广泛应用。方法上提出了符号奖励机器及其学习算法QSRM和LSRM，通过符号公式作为守卫直接处理环境原始观测，无需预定义标签。主要实验结果表明，SRM方法在性能上优于基线强化学习方法，并与现有RM方法结果相当，同时遵循广泛使用的环境定义，为用户提供了可解释的任务表示。
QFlowNet: Fast, Diverse, and Efficient Unitary Synthesis with Generative Flow Networks
Authors: Inhoe Koo, Hyunho Cha, Jungwoo Lee
First: 2026-03-03T14:38:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T14:38:05+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 6 figures, IEEE International Conference on Quantum Communications, Networking, and Computing (QCNC 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unitary Synthesis, the decomposition of a unitary matrix into a sequence of quantum gates, is a fundamental challenge in quantum compilation. Prevailing reinforcement learning(RL) approaches are often hampered by sparse reward signals, which necessitate complex reward shaping or long training times, and typically converge to a single policy, lacking solution diversity. In this work, we propose QFlowNet, a novel framework that learns efficiently from sparse signals by pairing a Generative Flow Network (GFlowNet) with Transformers. Our approach addresses two key challenges. First, the GFlowNet framework is fundamentally designed to learn a diverse policy that samples solutions proportional to their reward, overcoming the single-solution limitation of RL while offering faster inference than other generative models like diffusion. Second, the Transformers act as a powerful encoder, capturing the non-local structure of unitary matrices and compressing a high-dimensional state into a dense latent representation for the policy network. Our agent achieves an overall success rate of 99.7% on a 3-qubit benchmark(lengths 1-12) and discovers a diverse set of compact circuits, establishing QFlowNet as an efficient and diverse paradigm for unitary synthesis.
中文标题/摘要
标题：QFlowNet：基于生成流网络的快速、多样、高效酉合成方法
酉合成——将酉矩阵分解为量子门序列——是量子编译中的核心挑战。现有强化学习方法常受稀疏奖励信号制约，需复杂奖励塑形或长时训练，且通常收敛至单一策略，缺乏解多样性。本文提出QFlowNet，通过将生成流网络与Transformer结合，实现从稀疏信号中高效学习的新框架。该方法解决两大关键问题：其一，GFlowNet框架本质设计为学习多样化策略，能按奖励比例采样解，克服强化学习的单解局限，且比扩散等生成模型推理更快；其二，Transformer作为强大编码器，捕捉酉矩阵的非局部结构，将高维状态压缩为策略网络的稠密隐表示。智能体在3量子比特基准测试（长度1-12）中达成99.7%总成功率，并发现多样紧凑电路，确立QFlowNet为高效且多样化的酉合成新范式。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces QFlowNet, a framework for unitary synthesis in quantum compilation, motivated by the limitations of existing reinforcement learning methods which suffer from sparse rewards and lack solution diversity. The method pairs a Generative Flow Network (GFlowNet) with Transformers, where the GFlowNet enables efficient learning from sparse signals and samples diverse solutions proportional to reward, while Transformers encode the non-local structure of unitary matrices into dense latent representations. Experimental results show a 99.7% success rate on a 3-qubit benchmark for circuit lengths 1-12, with the discovery of diverse, compact circuits, demonstrating QFlowNet's efficiency and diversity.
本文提出了QFlowNet框架，用于量子编译中的酉合成，其动机是现有强化学习方法存在奖励稀疏和缺乏解多样性的问题。该方法将生成流网络（GFlowNet）与Transformer结合，其中GFlowNet能从稀疏奖励中高效学习并采样与奖励成正比的多样化解，而Transformer则将酉矩阵的非局部结构编码为密集潜在表示。实验结果表明，在3量子比特基准测试（长度1-12）上实现了99.7%的整体成功率，并发现了多样化的紧凑电路，证明了QFlowNet的高效性和多样性。
Learning Acrobatic Flight from Preferences
Authors: Colin Merk, Ismail Geles, Jiaxu Xing, Angel Romero, Giorgia Ramponi, Davide Scaramuzza
First: 2025-08-26T08:56:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T14:35:14+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Preference-based reinforcement learning (PbRL) enables agents to learn control policies without requiring manually designed reward functions, making it well-suited for tasks where objectives are difficult to formalize or inherently subjective. Acrobatic flight poses a particularly challenging problem due to its complex dynamics, rapid movements, and the importance of precise execution. However, manually designed reward functions for such tasks often fail to capture the qualities that matter: we find that hand-crafted rewards agree with human judgment only 60.7% of the time, underscoring the need for preference-driven approaches. In this work, we propose Reward Ensemble under Confidence (REC), a probabilistic reward learning framework for PbRL that explicitly models per-timestep reward uncertainty through an ensemble of distributional reward models. By propagating uncertainty into the preference loss and leveraging disagreement for exploration, REC achieves 88.4% of shaped reward performance on acrobatic quadrotor control, compared to 55.2% with standard Preference PPO. We train policies in simulation and successfully transfer them zero-shot to the real world, demonstrating complex acrobatic maneuvers learned purely from preference feedback. We further validate REC on a continuous control benchmark, confirming its applicability beyond the domain of aerial robotics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于偏好的特技飞行学习
基于偏好的强化学习（PbRL）使智能体无需手动设计奖励函数即可学习控制策略，这使其特别适用于目标难以形式化或具有主观性的任务。特技飞行因其复杂的动力学特性、快速运动及精确执行的重要性而构成一项极具挑战性的问题。然而，针对此类任务手动设计的奖励函数往往难以捕捉关键质量特征：我们发现人工设计的奖励与人类判断的一致性仅为60.7%，这凸显了偏好驱动方法的必要性。本研究提出置信度下的奖励集成（REC）——一种用于PbRL的概率奖励学习框架，通过分布奖励模型集成显式建模每时间步的奖励不确定性。通过将不确定性传播至偏好损失函数并利用分歧进行探索，REC在特技四旋翼控制任务中达到人工设计奖励性能的88.4%，而标准偏好PPO仅达到55.2%。我们在仿真环境中训练策略，并成功零样本迁移至现实世界，展示了完全通过偏好反馈学习的复杂特技飞行动作。我们还在连续控制基准测试中进一步验证了REC，证实了其超越空中机器人领域的适用性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that manually designing reward functions for complex tasks like acrobatic flight is difficult and often misaligned with human judgment, with hand-crafted rewards agreeing only 60.7% of the time. To address this, the authors propose Reward Ensemble under Confidence (REC), a preference-based reinforcement learning method that models reward uncertainty using an ensemble of distributional reward models and incorporates this uncertainty into the preference loss to guide exploration. Experimental results show that REC achieves 88.4% of the performance of a shaped reward on acrobatic quadrotor control, significantly outperforming standard Preference PPO at 55.2%, and successfully transfers learned policies zero-shot from simulation to real-world drones, enabling complex maneuvers learned purely from preferences.
本研究的动机在于，为复杂任务（如特技飞行）手动设计奖励函数非常困难，且常与人类判断不一致，手工奖励的符合率仅为60.7%。为此，作者提出了置信度下的奖励集成方法，这是一种基于偏好的强化学习方法，通过集成分布奖励模型来建模奖励不确定性，并将不确定性融入偏好损失中以指导探索。实验结果表明，该方法在特技四旋翼控制任务中达到了手工设计奖励性能的88.4%，显著优于标准偏好PPO的55.2%，并成功将策略从仿真零样本迁移到真实无人机上，实现了仅通过偏好反馈学习复杂飞行动作。
Why Does RLAIF Work At All?
Authors: Robin Young
First: 2026-03-03T13:51:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:51:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF) enables language models to improve by training on their own preference judgments, yet no theoretical account explains why this self-improvement seemingly works for value learning. We propose the latent value hypothesis, that pretraining on internet-scale data encodes human values as directions in representation space, and constitutional prompts elicit these latent values into preference judgments. We formalize this intuition under a linear model where the constitution acts as a projection operator selecting value-relevant directions. Our analysis yields several results. RLAIF improves alignment when the constitution-activated direction correlates with true values better than the model's default generation direction thus explaining the generation-judgment gap; the ceiling on RLAIF quality is determined by how well representations encode values, which scales with model capacity; and adversarial constitutions exist that can activate anti-social value directions encoded from harmful pretraining data. Our account unifies scattered empirical findings including the refusal direction, low-rank safety subspaces, and RLAIF scaling behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLAIF为何有效？
基于人工智能反馈的强化学习（RLAIF）使语言模型能通过自身偏好判断进行训练以提升性能，但尚无理论解释这种自我改进为何在价值学习中有效。我们提出潜在价值假说：互联网规模数据的预训练将人类价值编码为表征空间中的方向，而宪法式提示将这些潜在价值激发为偏好判断。在线性模型框架下，我们将此直觉形式化，将宪法视为选择价值相关方向的投影算子。分析得出多项结论：当宪法激活的方向比模型默认生成方向更贴合真实价值时，RLAIF能提升对齐性，这解释了生成与判断的差距；RLAIF的质量上限取决于表征编码价值的程度，其随模型能力扩展；存在对抗性宪法可激活从有害预训练数据中编码的反社会价值方向。本理论统一了包括拒绝方向、低秩安全子空间及RLAIF扩展规律在内的多项实证发现。

The authors propose the latent value hypothesis, which posits that pretraining embeds human values as directions in representation space, and constitutional prompts act as projection operators to elicit these latent values for judgment. Under a linear model formalization, their analysis shows that RLAIF improves alignment when the constitution-activated direction better correlates with true values than the default generation direction, explains the generation-judgment gap, establishes that quality ceilings depend on how well representations encode values (scaling with model capacity), and reveals that adversarial constitutions can activate harmful value directions from pretraining data. This account unifies empirical observations like refusal directions and RLAIF scaling behavior.
本文的动机在于缺乏理论解释为何基于人工智能反馈的强化学习（RLAIF）能通过模型自身的偏好判断有效实现自我改进。作者提出了潜在价值假说，认为预训练将人类价值编码为表示空间中的方向，而宪法提示作为投影算子来激发这些潜在价值以进行判断。在线性模型形式化下，分析表明当宪法激活的方向比默认生成方向更贴合真实价值时，RLAIF能提升对齐性，从而解释了生成与判断之间的差距；其质量上限取决于表示编码价值的效果（随模型能力扩展），且对抗性宪法可能激活预训练数据中的有害价值方向。该理论统一了包括拒绝方向、低秩安全子空间和RLAIF扩展行为在内的多项实证发现。
Contextualized Privacy Defense for LLM Agents
Authors: Yule Wen, Yanzhe Zhang, Jianxun Lian, Xiaoyuan Yi, Xing Xie, Diyi Yang
First: 2026-03-03T13:35:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:35:33+00:00
Comments: 25 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM agents increasingly act on users' personal information, yet existing privacy defenses remain limited in both design and adaptability. Most prior approaches rely on static or passive defenses, such as prompting and guarding. These paradigms are insufficient for supporting contextual, proactive privacy decisions in multi-step agent execution. We propose Contextualized Defense Instructing (CDI), a new privacy defense paradigm in which an instructor model generates step-specific, context-aware privacy guidance during execution, proactively shaping actions rather than merely constraining or vetoing them. Crucially, CDI is paired with an experience-driven optimization framework that trains the instructor via reinforcement learning (RL), where we convert failure trajectories with privacy violations into learning environments. We formalize baseline defenses and CDI as distinct intervention points in a canonical agent loop, and compare their privacy-helpfulness trade-offs within a unified simulation framework. Results show that our CDI consistently achieves a better balance between privacy preservation (94.2%) and helpfulness (80.6%) than baselines, with superior robustness to adversarial conditions and generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大语言模型智能体的情境化隐私防御
大语言模型智能体日益频繁地处理用户个人信息，但现有隐私防御机制在设计和适应性方面均存在局限。多数现有方法依赖静态或被动的防御策略，如提示与防护机制。这些范式难以支持多步骤智能体执行过程中情境化、主动式的隐私决策。本文提出情境化防御指导（CDI）这一新型隐私防御范式：通过指导模型在执行过程中生成针对具体步骤、感知情境的隐私指引，主动塑造智能体行为而非仅进行约束或否决。关键创新在于，CDI配套构建了经验驱动的优化框架，通过强化学习训练指导模型——将包含隐私违规的失败轨迹转化为学习环境。我们在规范智能体循环中形式化定义了基线防御与CDI作为不同的干预节点，并在统一仿真框架内比较其隐私保护与助益性的权衡关系。实验表明，CDI在隐私保护率（94.2%）与助益性（80.6%）之间始终取得优于基线方法的平衡，且对对抗性条件与泛化场景表现出更强的鲁棒性。

The method employs a reinforcement learning framework to train the instructor by converting failure trajectories with privacy violations into learning environments, optimizing for step-specific interventions. Experimental results within a unified simulation framework demonstrate that CDI achieves a superior balance, with 94.2% privacy preservation and 80.6% helpfulness, outperforming baselines in robustness and generalization.
针对大语言模型代理处理个人信息时静态隐私防御的不足，本文提出了情境化防御指导（CDI）范式，通过一个指导模型在代理执行过程中主动生成情境感知的隐私指导。该方法采用强化学习框架训练指导模型，将包含隐私违规的失败轨迹转化为学习环境，以优化针对具体步骤的干预。在统一模拟框架内的实验结果表明，CDI在隐私保护（94.2%）和帮助性（80.6%）之间取得了更优的平衡，其鲁棒性和泛化能力均优于基线方法。
LAGO: A Local-Global Optimization Framework Combining Trust Region Methods and Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Eliott Van Dieren, Tommaso Vanzan, Fabio Nobile
First: 2026-03-03T13:24:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:24:36+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce LAGO, a LocAl-Global Optimization algorithm that combines gradient-enhanced Bayesian Optimization (BO) with gradient-based trust region local refinement through an adaptive competition mechanism. At each iteration, global and local optimization strategies independently propose candidate points, and the next evaluation is selected based on predicted improvement. LAGO separates global exploration from local refinement at the proposal level: the BO acquisition function is optimized outside the active trust region, while local function and gradient evaluations are incorporated into the global gradient-enhanced Gaussian process only when they satisfy a lengthscale-based minimum-distance criterion, reducing the risk of numerical instability during the local exploitation. This enables efficient local refinement when reaching promising regions, without sacrificing a global search of the design space. As a result, the method achieves an improved exploration of the full design space compared to standard non-linear local optimization algorithms for smooth functions, while maintaining fast local convergence in regions of interest.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LAGO：融合信赖域方法与贝叶斯优化的局部-全局优化框架
本文提出LAGO算法，一种通过自适应竞争机制将梯度增强贝叶斯优化与基于梯度的信赖域局部优化相结合的局部-全局优化方法。每次迭代中，全局与局部优化策略独立生成候选点，并根据预测改进值选择评估点。LAGO在提案层面分离全局探索与局部优化：贝叶斯采集函数在活跃信赖域外优化，而局部函数与梯度评估仅当满足基于长度尺度的最小距离准则时才纳入全局梯度增强高斯过程，从而降低局部开发时的数值不稳定风险。该方法在抵达潜力区域时可实现高效局部优化，同时不牺牲设计空间的全局搜索能力。相较于标准非线性局部优化算法，本方法在平滑函数上实现了更全面的设计空间探索，并在关注区域保持快速局部收敛。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LAGO, a hybrid optimization framework motivated by the need to efficiently balance global exploration and local refinement for smooth functions, overcoming the limitations of purely local or global methods. The method combines gradient-enhanced Bayesian Optimization for global search with a trust region method for local refinement, using an adaptive competition mechanism where both strategies propose candidates and the next evaluation is selected based on predicted improvement; it strategically separates global and local proposals and incorporates local evaluations into the global model only when a lengthscale-based criterion is met to ensure numerical stability. Experimental results demonstrate that LAGO achieves improved global exploration compared to standard nonlinear local optimizers while maintaining fast local convergence in promising regions, as validated through benchmarks.
本文提出了LAGO混合优化框架，其动机在于需要高效平衡光滑函数的全局探索与局部优化，以克服纯局部或全局方法的局限。该方法将梯度增强的贝叶斯优化用于全局搜索，并结合信赖域方法进行局部优化，通过一种自适应竞争机制让两种策略分别提出候选点，并根据预测改进选择下一次评估；它策略性地分离全局与局部提议，并仅当满足基于长度尺度的最小距离准则时才将局部评估纳入全局模型，以确保数值稳定性。实验结果表明，与标准的非线性局部优化器相比，LAGO在保持感兴趣区域快速局部收敛的同时，实现了对设计空间更优的全局探索，这通过基准测试得到了验证。
Near-Constant Strong Violation and Last-Iterate Convergence for Online CMDPs via Decaying Safety Margins
Authors: Qian Zuo, Zhiyong Wang, Fengxiang He
First: 2026-02-11T14:54:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:11:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study safe online reinforcement learning in Constrained Markov Decision Processes (CMDPs) under strong regret and violation metrics, which forbid error cancellation over time. Existing primal-dual methods that achieve sublinear strong reward regret inevitably incur growing strong constraint violation or are restricted to average-iterate convergence due to inherent oscillations. To address these limitations, we propose the Flexible safety Domain Optimization via Margin-regularized Exploration (FlexDOME) algorithm, the first to provably achieve near-constant $\tilde{O}(1)$ strong constraint violation alongside sublinear strong regret and non-asymptotic last-iterate convergence. FlexDOME incorporates time-varying safety margins and regularization terms into the primal-dual framework. Our theoretical analysis relies on a novel term-wise asymptotic dominance strategy, where the safety margin is rigorously scheduled to asymptotically majorize the functional decay rates of the optimization and statistical errors, thereby clamping cumulative violations to a near-constant level. Furthermore, we establish non-asymptotic last-iterate convergence guarantees via a policy-dual Lyapunov argument. Experiments corroborate our theoretical findings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于衰减安全裕度的在线约束马尔可夫决策过程：近恒定强违反与末次迭代收敛
本研究在强遗憾和强违反度量下探索约束马尔可夫决策过程中的安全在线强化学习，该度量禁止误差随时间抵消。现有实现次线性强奖励遗憾的原对偶方法，由于固有振荡性，必然导致增长的强约束违反或仅限于平均迭代收敛。为突破这些局限，我们提出基于裕度正则化探索的柔性安全域优化算法，该算法首次可证明地实现近恒定$\tilde{O}(1)$强约束违反，同时保持次线性强遗憾与非渐近末次迭代收敛。该算法将时变安全裕度与正则化项融入原对偶框架。理论分析依托新颖的逐项渐近主导策略：通过严格调度安全裕度使其渐近主导优化误差与统计误差的函数衰减率，从而将累积违反控制在近恒定水平。此外，我们通过策略-对偶李雅普诺夫论证建立了非渐近末次迭代收敛保证。实验数据验证了理论结论。

This paper addresses the limitations of existing primal-dual methods for safe online reinforcement learning in Constrained Markov Decision Processes (CMDPs), which often suffer from growing strong constraint violation or only achieve average-iterate convergence. The authors propose the FlexDOME algorithm, which integrates time-varying safety margins and regularization into the primal-dual framework to rigorously control cumulative errors. The main experimental results demonstrate that FlexDOME provably achieves near-constant strong constraint violation alongside sublinear strong regret and guarantees non-asymptotic last-iterate convergence, as supported by both theoretical analysis and empirical validation.
本文针对现有原始对偶方法在约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP）安全在线强化学习中存在的强约束违反增长或仅实现平均迭代收敛的局限性，提出了FlexDOME算法。该方法通过在原始对偶框架中引入时变安全裕度和正则化项，以严格控制累积误差。主要实验结果表明，FlexDOME可证明地实现了近乎恒定的强约束违反，同时具有次线性强遗憾，并保证了非渐近的最后迭代收敛性，理论分析和实验均验证了这些发现。
CGL: Advancing Continual GUI Learning via Reinforcement Fine-Tuning
Authors: Zhenquan Yao, Zitong Huang, Yihan Zeng, Jianhua Han, Hang Xu, Chun-Mei Feng, Jianwei Ma, Wangmeng Zuo
First: 2026-03-03T13:02:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:02:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graphical User Interface (GUI) Agents, benefiting from recent advances in multimodal large language models (MLLM), have achieved significant development. However, due to the frequent updates of GUI applications, adapting to new tasks without forgetting old tasks in GUI continual learning remains an open problem. In this work, we reveal that while Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) facilitates fast adaptation, it often triggers knowledge overwriting, whereas Reinforcement Learning (RL) demonstrates an inherent resilience that shields prior interaction logic from erasure. Based on this insight, we propose a \textbf{C}ontinual \textbf{G}UI \textbf{L}earning (CGL) framework that dynamically balances adaptation efficiency and skill retention by enhancing the synergy between SFT and RL. Specifically, we introduce an SFT proportion adjustment mechanism guided by policy entropy to dynamically control the weight allocation between the SFT and RL training phases. To resolve explicit gradient interference, we further develop a specialized gradient surgery strategy. By projecting exploratory SFT gradients onto GRPO-based anchor gradients, our method explicitly clips the components of SFT gradients that conflict with GRPO. On top of that, we establish an AndroidControl-CL benchmark, which divides GUI applications into distinct task groups to effectively simulate and evaluate the performance of continual GUI learning. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of our proposed CGL framework across continual learning scenarios. The benchmark, code, and model will be made publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CGL：通过强化微调推进持续GUI学习
得益于多模态大语言模型（MLLM）的最新进展，图形用户界面（GUI）智能体取得了显著发展。然而，由于GUI应用频繁更新，如何在持续学习中适应新任务而不遗忘旧任务仍是一个开放性问题。本研究揭示：监督微调（SFT）虽能促进快速适应，但常引发知识覆盖；而强化学习（RL）则展现出内在韧性，能保护既有交互逻辑免遭擦除。基于此洞见，我们提出持续GUI学习（CGL）框架，通过增强SFT与RL的协同作用，动态平衡适应效率与技能保留。具体而言，我们引入基于策略熵的SFT比例调节机制，动态控制SFT与RL训练阶段的权重分配。为解决显式梯度干扰，进一步开发专用梯度手术策略：通过将探索性SFT梯度投影至基于GRPO的锚定梯度，显式裁剪与GRPO冲突的SFT梯度分量。此外，我们构建了AndroidControl-CL基准测试，将GUI应用划分为独立任务组以有效模拟和评估持续GUI学习性能。实验结果表明，所提CGL框架在持续学习场景中具有显著有效性。基准测试、代码与模型将公开提供。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of continual learning for GUI agents, where adapting to new application updates often leads to catastrophic forgetting of previously learned tasks. The authors propose a Continual GUI Learning (CGL) framework that dynamically balances adaptation and retention by synergizing Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL), incorporating an SFT proportion adjustment mechanism guided by policy entropy and a gradient surgery strategy to mitigate interference between SFT and RL gradients. Experiments on the newly introduced AndroidControl-CL benchmark demonstrate that CGL effectively maintains performance across sequential tasks, outperforming methods that rely solely on SFT or RL.
本文针对图形用户界面（GUI）智能体在持续学习中的挑战，即适应新应用更新时容易遗忘旧任务的问题，提出了一种持续GUI学习（CGL）框架。该方法通过结合监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL），引入基于策略熵的SFT比例调整机制和梯度手术策略，以动态平衡学习效率与技能保留，并减少梯度冲突。在新构建的AndroidControl-CL基准测试上的实验结果表明，CGL框架在连续任务场景中有效提升了性能，优于单独使用SFT或RL的方法。
Beyond One-Size-Fits-All: Adaptive Subgraph Denoising for Zero-Shot Graph Learning with Large Language Models
Authors: Fengzhi Li, Liang Zhang, Yuan Zuo, Ruiqing Zhao, YanSong Liu, Yunfei Ma, Fanyu Meng, Junlan Feng
First: 2026-03-03T12:47:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:47:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graph-based tasks in the zero-shot setting remain a significant challenge due to data scarcity and the inability of traditional Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) to generalize to unseen domains or label spaces. While recent advancements have transitioned toward leveraging Large Language Models (LLMs) as predictors to enhance GNNs, these methods often suffer from cross-modal alignment issues. A recent paradigm (i.e., Graph-R1) overcomes the aforementioned architectural dependencies by adopting a purely text-based format and utilizing LLM-based graph reasoning, showing improved zero-shot generalization. However, it employs a task-agnostic, one-size-fits-all subgraph extraction strategy, which inevitably introduces significant structural noise--irrelevant neighbors and edges--that distorts the LLMs' receptive field and leads to suboptimal predictions. To address this limitation, we introduce GraphSSR, a novel framework designed for adaptive subgraph extraction and denoising in zero-shot LLM-based graph reasoning. Specifically, we propose the SSR pipeline, which dynamically tailors subgraph extraction to specific contexts through a "Sample-Select-Reason" process, enabling the model to autonomously filter out task-irrelevant neighbors and overcome the one-size-fits-all issue. To internalize this capability, we develop SSR-SFT, a data synthesis strategy that generates high-quality SSR-style graph reasoning traces for supervised fine-tuning of LLMs. Furthermore, we propose SSR-RL, a two-stage reinforcement learning framework that explicitly regulates sampling and selection operations within the proposed SSR pipeline designed for adaptive subgraph denoising. By incorporating Authenticity-Reinforced and Denoising-Reinforced RL, we guide the model to achieve accurate predictions using parsimonious, denoised subgraphs for reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越通用范式：面向大语言模型零样本图学习的自适应子图去噪
零样本场景下的图学习任务因数据稀缺及传统图神经网络（GNN）难以泛化至未见领域或标签空间而面临严峻挑战。尽管近期研究转向利用大语言模型（LLM）作为预测器增强GNN，这些方法常受跨模态对齐问题制约。新兴范式Graph-R1通过采用纯文本格式与基于LLM的图推理，突破了前述架构依赖，展现出更优的零样本泛化能力。然而，其采用的任务无关通用子图提取策略会引入显著结构噪声（无关邻接节点与边），扭曲LLM的感知域并导致次优预测。为此，我们提出GraphSSR框架，专为零样本LLM图推理设计自适应子图提取与去噪机制。具体而言，我们构建SSR流程，通过“采样-选择-推理”三阶段动态定制上下文相关子图，使模型能自主过滤任务无关邻接节点，突破通用化局限。为内化此能力，我们开发SSR-SFT数据合成策略，生成高质量SSR式图推理轨迹用于LLM监督微调。进一步提出SSR-RL两阶段强化学习框架，在SSR流程中显式调控采样与选择操作以实现自适应子图去噪。通过融合真实性强化与去噪强化机制，引导模型使用精简去噪子图达成精准推理预测。

Experimental results demonstrate that GraphSSR effectively reduces structural noise and improves zero-shot prediction performance compared to existing methods.

Contextual Latent World Models for Offline Meta Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mohammadreza Nakheai, Aidan Scannell, Kevin Luck, Joni Pajarinen
First: 2026-03-03T12:45:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:45:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline meta-reinforcement learning seeks to learn policies that generalize across related tasks from fixed datasets. Context-based methods infer a task representation from transition histories, but learning effective task representations without supervision remains a challenge. In parallel, latent world models have demonstrated strong self-supervised representation learning through temporal consistency. We introduce contextual latent world models, which condition latent world models on inferred task representations and train them jointly with the context encoder. This enforces task-conditioned temporal consistency, yielding task representations that capture task-dependent dynamics rather than merely discriminating between tasks. Our method learns more expressive task representations and significantly improves generalization to unseen tasks across MuJoCo, Contextual-DeepMind Control, and Meta-World benchmarks.

On the Structural Limitations of Weight-Based Neural Adaptation and the Role of Reversible Behavioral Learning
Authors: Pardhu Sri Rushi Varma Konduru
First: 2026-03-03T12:44:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:44:12+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 5 figures. Preprint version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural models are usually adapted through changes in parameters shared among model components via fine-tuning, alignment-based training, and reinforcement learning. These changes have been found effective in short-term optimization. However, they result in long-term alterations in the model's base behavior. In this study, we introduce the concept of structural irreversibility as a characteristic of shared-parameter model adaptation. This concept refers to the intertwining of task-specific objectives with the representational identity of the model. We show that when parameters are directly mutated, the resulting model behaves divergently from the original model. This divergence cannot be reversed deterministically without an explicit parameter snapshot. We introduce reversible behavioral learning, in which model behaviors are structurally dissociated from identity parameters and can be deterministically unloaded through an explicit unload process. We also introduce the Recoverability Factor as a normalized measure of behavioral recoverability and provide additional diagnostics based on model divergence. Experiments show that reversible model adaptation achieves rollback within numerical precision, whereas shared-parameter mutation exhibits persistent post-reset divergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：论基于权重的神经适应的结构局限性及可逆行为学习的作用
神经模型通常通过微调、基于对齐的训练和强化学习等方式，改变模型组件间共享的参数来实现适应。这些改变在短期优化中被证明有效，但会导致模型基础行为的长期改变。本研究引入结构不可逆性作为共享参数模型适应的特征概念，指任务特定目标与模型表征身份的相互交织。研究表明，当参数被直接修改时，所得模型的行为会偏离原始模型，且若无明确的参数快照，这种偏离无法确定性逆转。我们提出可逆行为学习，将模型行为与身份参数在结构上解耦，可通过显式卸载过程确定性移除。同时引入可恢复性因子作为行为可恢复性的标准化度量，并提供基于模型偏离的额外诊断。实验表明，可逆模型适应能在数值精度内实现回滚，而共享参数突变则表现出重置后的持续偏离。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the structural limitations of conventional neural network adaptation methods like fine-tuning, which permanently alter a model's base behavior due to shared parameter updates, a phenomenon termed structural irreversibility. To address this, the authors propose reversible behavioral learning, a method that structurally dissociates learned behaviors from the model's core identity parameters, enabling deterministic unloading of behaviors without a parameter snapshot. Experimental results demonstrate that this reversible adaptation achieves precise behavioral rollback within numerical precision, whereas standard weight-based mutation leads to persistent divergence even after reset attempts, as quantified by their introduced Recoverability Factor and divergence diagnostics.
本文研究了传统神经网络适应方法（如微调）的结构性局限，这些方法由于共享参数的更新会永久改变模型的基础行为，这一现象被称为结构不可逆性。为解决该问题，作者提出了可逆行为学习方法，该方法将学习到的行为与模型核心身份参数在结构上解耦，从而无需参数快照即可确定性地卸载行为。实验结果表明，这种可逆适应能在数值精度内实现精确的行为回滚，而标准的基于权重的突变即使在重置后仍会导致持续的行为差异，这通过其引入的可恢复性因子和差异诊断指标得到了量化验证。
Learning to Evolve for Optimization via Stability-Inducing Neural Unrolling
Authors: Jiaxin Gao, Yaohua Liu, Ran Cheng, Kay Chen Tan
First: 2025-12-12T10:46:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:41:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Evolutionary algorithms serve as a powerful paradigm for tackling optimization challenges, yet their reliance on manually engineered heuristics inherently limits their adaptability across diverse landscapes. However, the transition from the hand-crafted heuristics to data-driven algorithms faces a fundamental dilemma: achieving neural \emph{plasticity} without sacrificing algorithmic stability. Although learned optimizers offer high adaptivity, their unconstrained update rules often result in unstable dynamics and brittle generalization on unseen landscapes. To address this challenge, this paper proposes Learning to Evolve (L2E), a bilevel meta-optimization framework that learns evolutionary search via stability-inducing neural unrolling. First, L2E reformulates population evolution as an unrolled fixed-point iteration via a structured neural operator. In this design, the inner loop imposes a stability-biased update structure, while the outer loop meta-trains the operator to produce effective search trajectories across tasks. Second, to balance global exploration with local refinement, a gradient-derived composite solver adaptively fuses learned evolutionary proposals with proxy numerical guidance in a differentiable manner. Extensive experiments on synthetic benchmarks and real-world control tasks demonstrate that L2E achieves substantial optimization performance, scales to high-dimensional problems, and exhibits robust zero-shot transfer across diverse test distributions.

标题：通过稳定性诱导神经展开实现优化进化的学习方法
进化算法作为解决优化挑战的强大范式，其依赖人工设计启发式规则的本质限制了在不同问题场景中的适应性。然而，从手工启发式转向数据驱动算法面临一个根本困境：如何在保持算法稳定性的前提下实现神经可塑性。尽管学习型优化器具有高适应性，但其无约束的更新规则常导致动态不稳定及在未见问题场景中的泛化脆弱性。为解决此问题，本文提出学习进化（L2E）框架——一种通过稳定性诱导神经展开学习进化搜索的双层元优化框架。首先，L2E通过结构化神经算子将种群进化重构为展开式定点迭代，其内层循环采用稳定性偏置的更新结构，外层循环则通过元训练使算子能跨任务生成有效搜索轨迹。其次，为平衡全局探索与局部优化，采用梯度导出的复合求解器以可微分方式自适应融合学习型进化方案与代理数值指导。在合成基准测试和实际控制任务上的大量实验表明，L2E能实现显著的优化性能，可扩展至高维问题，并在多样化测试分布中展现出强大的零样本迁移能力。

The proposed method, Learning to Evolve (L2E), introduces a bilevel meta-optimization framework that unrolls population evolution as a fixed-point iteration via a structured neural operator, with an inner loop enforcing stability-biased updates and an outer loop meta-training the operator for effective search across tasks; it also incorporates a gradient-derived composite solver to adaptively fuse learned evolutionary proposals with numerical guidance for balanced exploration and refinement. Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference with Conditional Lagrangian Optimal Transport
Authors: Harry Amad, Mihaela van der Schaar
First: 2026-03-02T11:55:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:35:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural networks (NNs) often have critical behavioural trade-offs that are set at design time with hyperparameters-such as reward weights in reinforcement learning or quantile targets in regression. Post-deployment, however, user preferences can evolve, making initial settings undesirable, necessitating potentially expensive retraining. To circumvent this, we introduce the task of Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference (HTI): to learn, from observed data, how a NN's conditional output distribution changes with its hyperparameters, and construct a surrogate model that approximates the NN at unobserved hyperparameter settings. HTI requires extending existing trajectory inference approaches to incorporate conditions, exacerbating the challenge of ensuring inferred paths are feasible. We propose an approach based on conditional Lagrangian optimal transport, jointly learning the Lagrangian function governing hyperparameter-induced dynamics along with the associated optimal transport maps and geodesics between observed marginals, which form the surrogate model. We incorporate inductive biases based on the manifold hypothesis and least-action principles into the learned Lagrangian, improving surrogate model feasibility. We empirically demonstrate that our approach reconstructs NN outputs across various hyperparameter spectra better than other alternatives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于条件拉格朗日最优传输的超参数轨迹推断
神经网络（NNs）常在设计时通过超参数（如强化学习中的奖励权重或回归中的分位数目标）设定关键行为权衡。然而，部署后用户偏好可能变化，导致初始设置不再适用，需进行可能昂贵的重新训练。为规避此问题，我们提出超参数轨迹推断（HTI）任务：从观测数据中学习NN的条件输出分布如何随超参数变化，并构建一个在未观测超参数设置下近似NN的代理模型。HTI需扩展现有轨迹推断方法以纳入条件，这加剧了确保推断路径可行的挑战。我们提出一种基于条件拉格朗日最优传输的方法，联合学习控制超参数诱导动态的拉格朗日函数，以及观测边缘分布间的最优传输映射和测地线（构成代理模型）。我们将基于流形假设和最小作用原理的归纳偏置融入学习的拉格朗日函数中，提升代理模型可行性。实验表明，我们的方法在多种超参数谱上重建NN输出的效果优于其他替代方案。

Enhancing Generative Auto-bidding with Offline Reward Evaluation and Policy Search
Authors: Zhiyu Mou, Yiqin Lv, Miao Xu, Qi Wang, Yixiu Mao, Jinghao Chen, Qichen Ye, Chao Li, Rongquan Bai, Chuan Yu, Jian Xu, Bo Zheng
First: 2025-09-19T12:30:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:29:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Auto-bidding is a critical tool for advertisers to improve advertising performance. Recent progress has demonstrated that AI-Generated Bidding (AIGB), which learns a conditional generative planner from offline data, achieves superior performance compared to typical offline reinforcement learning (RL)-based auto-bidding methods. However, existing AIGB methods still face a performance bottleneck due to their inherent inability to explore beyond the static dataset with feedback. To address this, we propose \textbf{AIGB-Pearl} (\emph{\textbf{P}lanning with \textbf{E}valu\textbf{A}tor via \textbf{RL}}), a novel method that integrates generative planning and policy optimization. The core of AIGB-Pearl lies in constructing a trajectory evaluator to assess the quality of generated scores and designing a provably sound KL-Lipschitz-constrained score-maximization scheme to ensure safe and efficient exploration beyond the offline dataset. A practical algorithm that incorporates the synchronous coupling technique is further developed to ensure the model regularity required by the proposed scheme. Extensive experiments on both simulated and real-world advertising systems demonstrate the state-of-the-art performance of our approach.

标题：通过离线奖励评估与策略搜索增强生成式自动出价

Experimental results on simulated and real-world advertising systems show that AIGB-Pearl achieves state-of-the-art performance.
本文针对基于静态离线数据的AI生成竞价方法因缺乏探索能力而面临的性能瓶颈问题，提出了一种名为AIGB-Pearl的新方法。该方法通过构建轨迹评估器来评估生成的竞价分数质量，并设计了一种可证明安全的KL-Lipschitz约束分数最大化方案，以实现对离线数据集之外的安全高效探索，同时结合同步耦合技术开发了实用算法。在模拟和真实广告系统上的大量实验表明，该方法取得了最先进的性能表现。
SAE as a Crystal Ball: Interpretable Features Predict Cross-domain Transferability of LLMs without Training
Authors: Qi Zhang, Yifei Wang, Xiaohan Wang, Jiajun Chai, Guojun Yin, Wei Lin, Yisen Wang
First: 2026-03-03T12:01:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:01:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In recent years, pre-trained large language models have achieved remarkable success across diverse tasks. Besides the pivotal role of self-supervised pre-training, their effectiveness in downstream applications also depends critically on the post-training process, which adapts models to task-specific data and objectives. However, this process inevitably introduces model shifts that can influence performance in different domains, and how such shifts transfer remains poorly understood. To open up the black box, we propose the SAE-based Transferability Score (STS), a new metric that leverages sparse autoencoders (SAEs) to forecast post-training transferability. Taking supervised fine-tuning as an example, STS identifies shifted dimensions in SAE representations and calculates their correlations with downstream domains, enabling reliable estimation of transferability \textit{before} fine-tuning. Extensive experiments across multiple models and domains show that STS accurately predicts the transferability of supervised fine-tuning, achieving Pearson correlation coefficients above 0.7 with actual performance changes. Beyond this, we take an initial step toward extending STS to reinforcement learning. We believe that STS can serve as an {\color{black} interpretable} tool for guiding post-training strategies in LLMs. Code is available at https://github.com/PKU-ML/STS.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SAE作为水晶球：可解释特征无需训练即可预测大语言模型的跨领域可迁移性
近年来，预训练大语言模型在多样化任务中取得了显著成功。除了自监督预训练的关键作用外，其在下游应用中的有效性还高度依赖于后训练过程，该过程使模型适应特定任务的数据与目标。然而，这一过程不可避免地引入可能影响不同领域性能的模型偏移，而此类偏移如何迁移仍鲜为人知。为揭示黑箱机制，我们提出基于稀疏自编码器的可迁移性评分（STS），这是一种利用稀疏自编码器预测后训练可迁移性的新指标。以监督微调为例，STS识别SAE表征中的偏移维度，并计算其与下游领域的相关性，从而能在微调前可靠估计可迁移性。跨多个模型与领域的广泛实验表明，STS能准确预测监督微调的可迁移性，与实际性能变化的皮尔逊相关系数超过0.7。此外，我们初步探索将STS扩展至强化学习。我们相信STS可作为一种可解释工具，用于指导大语言模型的后训练策略。代码发布于https://github.com/PKU-ML/STS。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand how post-training adaptations like fine-tuning affect large language models' performance across different domains, this paper introduces the SAE-based Transferability Score (STS), a method that uses sparse autoencoders to analyze feature shifts in model representations and predict transferability before actual training. The approach correlates these shifted dimensions with target domains to estimate performance changes, with experiments on multiple models and domains demonstrating that STS achieves high predictive accuracy, showing Pearson correlations above 0.7 with real performance shifts, and it is also preliminarily extended to reinforcement learning scenarios.
本文旨在解决大型语言模型在微调等后训练过程中性能跨领域迁移性难以预测的问题，提出了一种基于稀疏自编码器的可迁移性评分方法。该方法通过分析模型表示中的特征维度变化，并与下游领域关联，从而在训练前预估迁移效果；实验表明，该方法在多个模型和领域上能准确预测监督微调的迁移性，与实际性能变化的皮尔逊相关系数超过0.7，并初步探索了在强化学习中的应用，为后训练策略提供了可解释的指导工具。
VideoTemp-o3: Harmonizing Temporal Grounding and Video Understanding in Agentic Thinking-with-Videos
Authors: Wenqi Liu, Yunxiao Wang, Shijie Ma, Meng Liu, Qile Su, Tianke Zhang, Haonan Fan, Changyi Liu, Kaiyu Jiang, Jiankang Chen, Kaiyu Tang, Bin Wen, Fan Yang, Tingting Gao, Han Li, Yinwei Wei, Xuemeng Song
First: 2026-02-08T03:45:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T11:46:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In long-video understanding, conventional uniform frame sampling often fails to capture key visual evidence, leading to degraded performance and increased hallucinations. To address this, recent agentic thinking-with-videos paradigms have emerged, adopting a localize-clip-answer pipeline in which the model actively identifies relevant video segments, performs dense sampling within those clips, and then produces answers. However, existing methods remain inefficient, suffer from weak localization, and adhere to rigid workflows. To solve these issues, we propose VideoTemp-o3, a unified agentic thinking-with-videos framework that jointly models video grounding and question answering. VideoTemp-o3 exhibits strong localization capability, supports on-demand clipping, and can refine inaccurate localizations. Specifically, in the supervised fine-tuning stage, we design a unified masking mechanism that encourages exploration while preventing noise. For reinforcement learning, we introduce dedicated rewards to mitigate reward hacking. Besides, from the data perspective, we develop an effective pipeline to construct high-quality long video grounded QA data, along with a corresponding benchmark for systematic evaluation across various video durations. Experimental results demonstrate that our method achieves remarkable performance on both long video understanding and grounding.

标题：VideoTemp-o3：在视频代理思维中协调时序定位与视频理解
在长视频理解中，传统的均匀帧采样常无法捕捉关键视觉证据，导致性能下降和幻觉增加。为解决此问题，近期出现了视频代理思维范式，采用定位-剪辑-回答流程，使模型主动识别相关视频片段、在片段内进行密集采样后生成答案。然而，现有方法效率低下、定位能力弱且依赖僵化流程。为此，我们提出VideoTemp-o3——一个统一视频代理思维框架，可联合建模视频定位与问答任务。该框架具备强定位能力，支持按需剪辑，并能修正不准确的定位结果。具体而言，在监督微调阶段，我们设计了统一的掩码机制以鼓励探索并抑制噪声；在强化学习中，引入专用奖励以缓解奖励攻击。此外，从数据层面构建了高质量长视频定位问答数据生成流程，并创建对应基准以系统评估不同时长视频。实验表明，本方法在长视频理解与定位任务上均取得显著性能提升。

Reducing Belief Deviation in Reinforcement Learning for Active Reasoning
Authors: Deyu Zou, Yongqiang Chen, Jianxiang Wang, Haochen Yang, Mufei Li, James Cheng, Pan Li, Yu Gong
Venue: ICLR 2026 Oral
First: 2025-10-14T08:14:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T11:42:46+00:00
Comments: Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026 (Oral)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Active reasoning requires large language model (LLM) agents to interact with external sources and strategically gather information to solve problems in multiple turns. Central to this process is belief tracking: maintaining an accurate representation of the underlying state and uncertainty in understanding and solving the problem. However, due to limited reasoning capabilities, LLM-based agents often suffer belief deviation: their internal beliefs drift from the true problem state, leading to loss of state awareness and uninformative or repetitive actions. Once this happens, errors compound in the trajectories used for reinforcement learning (RL), leading to misattributed credits and limited exploration. To address this issue, we propose to track belief deviation and develop $\mathbf{T^3}$, a simple yet principled method that detects excessive deviation and truncates training trajectories to suppress uninformative tail effects. Hence, $\mathbf{T^3}$ preserves credits for informative prefixes and systematically improves policy optimization. Across 5 challenging tasks, $\mathbf{T^3}$ consistently enhances training stability and yields performance gains of up to 30 points while cutting token cost by up to 34%. These results highlight belief control as a key principle for building robust LLM agents capable of active reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中减少信念偏差以促进主动推理
主动推理要求大语言模型（LLM）智能体与外部源交互，并通过多轮策略性信息收集来解决问题。该过程的核心是信念追踪：保持对底层状态及问题理解与求解中不确定性的准确表征。然而，由于推理能力有限，基于LLM的智能体常出现信念偏差：其内部信念偏离真实问题状态，导致状态感知丧失并产生无信息量或重复的行动。一旦发生这种情况，用于强化学习（RL）的轨迹中误差会不断累积，造成信用分配错误并限制探索。为解决此问题，我们提出追踪信念偏差并开发了$\mathbf{T^3}$方法——一种简洁而原则性的方法，可检测过度偏差并截断训练轨迹以抑制无信息量的尾部效应。因此，$\mathbf{T^3}$能保留信息丰富的前缀段信用，系统性地改进策略优化。在5项挑战性任务中，$\mathbf{T^3}$持续提升训练稳定性，实现高达30个百分点的性能增益，同时降低最多34%的令牌成本。这些结果凸显了信念控制作为构建具备主动推理能力的鲁棒LLM智能体的关键原则。

Learning in Markov Decision Processes with Exogenous Dynamics
Authors: Davide Maran, Davide Salaorni, Marcello Restelli
First: 2026-03-03T11:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T11:10:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning algorithms are typically designed for generic Markov Decision Processes (MDPs), where any state-action pair can lead to an arbitrary transition distribution. In many practical systems, however, only a subset of the state variables is directly influenced by the agent's actions, while the remaining components evolve according to exogenous dynamics and account for most of the stochasticity. In this work, we study a structured class of MDPs characterized by exogenous state components whose transitions are independent of the agent's actions. We show that exploiting this structure yields significantly improved learning guarantees, with only the size of the exogenous state space appearing in the leading terms of the regret bounds. We further establish a matching lower bound, showing that this dependence is information-theoretically optimal. Finally, we empirically validate our approach across classical toy settings and real-world-inspired environments, demonstrating substantial gains in sample efficiency compared to standard reinforcement learning methods.

标题：具有外生动态的马尔可夫决策过程学习
强化学习算法通常为通用马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）设计，其中任意状态-动作对可导致任意转移分布。然而，在许多实际系统中，仅部分状态变量直接受智能体动作影响，其余部分则按外生动态演化并构成随机性的主要来源。本研究针对一类具有外生状态分量的结构化MDP展开分析，其转移过程独立于智能体动作。我们证明利用该结构可显著提升学习保证，仅外生状态空间规模出现在遗憾边界的主导项中。进一步建立匹配下界，表明该依赖关系在信息论意义下最优。最后，通过在经典玩具场景和现实启发环境中进行实证验证，相比标准强化学习方法，本方法在样本效率上展现出显著优势。

Learning Memory-Enhanced Improvement Heuristics for Flexible Job Shop Scheduling
Authors: Jiaqi Wang, Zhiguang Cao, Peng Zhao, Rui Cao, Yubin Xiao, Yuan Jiang, You Zhou
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2026-03-03T10:43:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T10:43:01+00:00
Comments: 39th Conference on Neural Information Processing Systems (NeurIPS 2025)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rise of smart manufacturing under Industry 4.0 introduces mass customization and dynamic production, demanding more advanced and flexible scheduling techniques. The flexible job-shop scheduling problem (FJSP) has attracted significant attention due to its complex constraints and strong alignment with real-world production scenarios. Current deep reinforcement learning (DRL)-based approaches to FJSP predominantly employ constructive methods. While effective, they often fall short of reaching (near-)optimal solutions. In contrast, improvement-based methods iteratively explore the neighborhood of initial solutions and are more effective in approaching optimality. However, the flexible machine allocation in FJSP poses significant challenges to the application of this framework, including accurate state representation, effective policy learning, and efficient search strategies. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a Memory-enhanced Improvement Search framework with heterogeneous graph representation--MIStar. It employs a novel heterogeneous disjunctive graph that explicitly models the operation sequences on machines to accurately represent scheduling solutions. Moreover, a memoryenhanced heterogeneous graph neural network (MHGNN) is designed for feature extraction, leveraging historical trajectories to enhance the decision-making capability of the policy network. Finally, a parallel greedy search strategy is adopted to explore the solution space, enabling superior solutions with fewer iterations. Extensive experiments on synthetic data and public benchmarks demonstrate that MIStar significantly outperforms both traditional handcrafted improvement heuristics and state-of-the-art DRL-based constructive methods.

标题：面向柔性作业车间调度的记忆增强型改进启发式方法学习
工业4.0下智能制造的兴起带来了大规模定制与动态生产，对更先进、灵活的调度技术提出了需求。柔性作业车间调度问题因其复杂约束和与现实生产场景的高度契合而备受关注。当前基于深度强化学习的柔性作业车间调度方法主要采用构造式方法，虽有效但常难以达到（近似）最优解。相比之下，基于改进的方法通过迭代探索初始解的邻域，能更有效地逼近最优解。然而，柔性作业车间调度中的机器柔性分配为该框架的应用带来了严峻挑战，包括精确的状态表示、有效的策略学习和高效的搜索策略。为应对这些挑战，本文提出一种基于异构图表示的记忆增强改进搜索框架——MIStar。该框架采用新型异质析取图，显式建模机器上的工序序列以精确表示调度方案；设计记忆增强异质图神经网络用于特征提取，利用历史轨迹提升策略网络的决策能力；并采用并行贪婪搜索策略探索解空间，以更少迭代获得更优解。在合成数据和公开基准上的大量实验表明，MIStar显著优于传统手工改进启发式方法和前沿的基于深度强化学习的构造式方法。

A Novel Evolutionary Method for Automated Skull-Face Overlay in Computer-Aided Craniofacial Superimposition
Authors: Práxedes Martínez-Moreno, Andrea Valsecchi, Pablo Mesejo, Pilar Navarro-Ramírez, Valentino Lugli, Sergio Damas
First: 2026-02-26T13:55:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T10:38:27+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 6 figures, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Craniofacial Superimposition is a forensic technique for identifying skeletal remains by comparing a post-mortem skull with ante-mortem facial photographs. A critical step in this process is Skull-Face Overlay (SFO). This stage involves aligning a 3D skull model with a 2D facial image, typically guided by cranial and facial landmarks' correspondence. However, its accuracy is undermined by individual variability in soft-tissue thickness, introducing significant uncertainty into the overlay. This paper introduces Lilium, an automated evolutionary method to enhance the accuracy and robustness of SFO. Lilium explicitly models soft-tissue variability using a 3D cone-based representation whose parameters are optimized via a Differential Evolution algorithm. The method enforces anatomical, morphological, and photographic plausibility through a combination of constraints: landmark matching, camera parameter consistency, head pose alignment, skull containment within facial boundaries, and region parallelism. This emulation of the usual forensic practitioners' approach leads Lilium to outperform the state-of-the-art method in terms of both accuracy and robustness.

标题：一种用于计算机辅助颅面叠加中自动颅骨-面部覆盖的新型进化方法
颅面叠加是一种法医学技术，通过比对死后颅骨与生前面部照片来识别骨骼遗骸。该过程中的关键步骤是颅骨-面部覆盖（SFO），涉及将三维颅骨模型与二维面部图像对齐，通常依据颅骨与面部标志点的对应关系进行。然而，软组织厚度的个体差异会降低其准确性，为覆盖过程引入显著不确定性。本文提出Lilium，一种自动进化方法，旨在提升SFO的准确性与鲁棒性。Lilium采用基于三维锥体的表示法明确建模软组织变异性，其参数通过差分进化算法优化。该方法结合多种约束条件确保解剖、形态及摄影合理性：标志点匹配、相机参数一致性、头部姿态对齐、颅骨包含于面部边界内以及区域平行性。通过模拟法医从业者的常规操作流程，Lilium在准确性和鲁棒性上均优于当前最优方法。

Benefits and Pitfalls of Reinforcement Learning for Language Model Planning: A Theoretical Perspective
Authors: Siwei Wang, Yifei Shen, Haoran Sun, Shi Feng, Shang-Hua Teng, Li Dong, Yaru Hao, Wei Chen
First: 2025-09-26T17:39:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T09:39:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent reinforcement learning (RL) methods have substantially enhanced the planning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), yet the theoretical basis for their effectiveness remains elusive. In this work, we investigate RL's benefits and limitations through a tractable graph-based abstraction, focusing on policy gradient (PG) and Q-learning methods. Our theoretical analyses reveal that supervised fine-tuning (SFT) may introduce co-occurrence-based spurious solutions, whereas RL achieves correct planning primarily through exploration, underscoring exploration's role in enabling better generalization. However, we also show that PG suffers from diversity collapse, where output diversity decreases during training and persists even after perfect accuracy is attained. By contrast, Q-learning provides two key advantages: off-policy learning and diversity preservation at convergence. We further demonstrate that careful reward design is necessary to prevent Q-value bias in Q-learning. Finally, applying our framework to the real-world planning benchmark Blocksworld, we confirm that these behaviors manifest in practice.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习在语言模型规划中的优势与陷阱：理论视角
近期强化学习方法显著提升了大型语言模型的规划能力，但其有效性的理论基础仍不明确。本研究通过可处理的图抽象框架，聚焦策略梯度和Q学习方法，探讨了强化学习的优势与局限。理论分析表明，监督微调可能引入基于共现的伪解，而强化学习主要通过探索实现正确规划，凸显了探索在提升泛化能力中的作用。然而，策略梯度方法存在多样性坍缩问题，即训练过程中输出多样性下降，且在达到完全准确后仍持续存在。相比之下，Q学习具有离策略学习和收敛时保持多样性两大优势。研究进一步证明，需精心设计奖励函数以避免Q学习中的Q值偏差。最后，在真实世界规划基准Blocksworld中应用本框架，验证了这些行为在实际中的显现。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand the theoretical underpinnings of reinforcement learning (RL) for enhancing language model planning, this paper analyzes RL's benefits and limitations using a graph-based abstraction, focusing on policy gradient and Q-learning methods. The method involves theoretical analyses revealing that supervised fine-tuning can lead to spurious co-occurrence solutions, while RL achieves correct planning through exploration, which aids generalization; however, policy gradient suffers from diversity collapse where output diversity diminishes even after perfect accuracy. In contrast, Q-learning offers advantages in off-policy learning and diversity preservation at convergence, though it requires careful reward design to avoid Q-value bias. Experimental results on the Blocksworld benchmark confirm these theoretical behaviors in practice.
本文旨在从理论角度探究强化学习在增强语言模型规划能力中的优势与局限，其动机在于理解强化学习有效性的理论基础。方法上，通过基于图的可处理抽象分析策略梯度和Q学习方法，理论分析表明监督微调可能引入基于共现的伪解，而强化学习主要通过探索实现正确规划，凸显了探索对泛化的作用；但策略梯度存在多样性崩溃问题，即训练中输出多样性下降且在达到完美精度后仍持续。相比之下，Q学习具有离策略学习和收敛时保持多样性的关键优势，但需精心设计奖励以避免Q值偏差。在Blocksworld实际规划基准上的实验结果验证了这些理论行为在实践中的表现。
Dynamic Deep-Reinforcement-Learning Algorithm in Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes
Authors: Saki Omi, Hyo-Sang Shin, Namhoon Cho, Antonios Tsourdos
First: 2023-07-29T08:52:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T09:28:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent studies have greatly improved reinforcement learning, and an increased interest in real-world implementation has emerged. In many cases, the implementation is challenged by time-varying disturbances as it introduces hidden states, which makes the problem best described with Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes. An effective approach to address this problem is to introduce a Recurrent Neural Network (RNN) in place of a state estimator. However, only a few studies have investigated the types of information to be supplied to the RNN and the network architecture to handle them. This study discusses the effectiveness of the inclusion of action along with observation and the impact of network architecture to handle them by providing interpretations of how the trajectories are summarized at LSTM networks. Specifically, three novel approaches with different architectures are introduced. All algorithms demonstrated the effectiveness of the inclusion of the action trajectories in simulation environments. In particular, one of the developed algorithms, H-TD3, differs from the typical actor and critic network as the critic network is trained by utilizing the hidden states generated by the actor network as the summarized trajectory information. This novel approach exhibited the potential improvement of the computational time while maintaining the performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程中的动态深度强化学习算法
近期研究显著推进了强化学习的发展，实际应用中的兴趣日益增长。然而，时变扰动常因引入隐藏状态而阻碍实施，使得问题更宜用部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程描述。一种有效解决方案是以循环神经网络替代状态估计器，但现有研究较少探讨应输入RNN的信息类型及处理这些信息的网络架构。本研究通过阐释LSTM网络如何汇总轨迹，探讨了在观测信息中加入动作的有效性及对应网络架构的影响，并提出三种具有不同架构的新方法。所有算法在仿真环境中均验证了纳入动作轨迹的有效性。其中，H-TD3算法采用创新设计：其评论家网络利用行动者网络生成的隐藏状态作为汇总轨迹信息进行训练，与传统行动者-评论家网络结构不同。该方法在保持性能的同时，展现出减少计算时间的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of applying reinforcement learning in real-world settings with time-varying disturbances and hidden states, which are best modeled as Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs), this paper investigates how to effectively incorporate action information alongside observations into Recurrent Neural Networks (RNNs) for state estimation. The method introduces three novel algorithmic architectures, including H-TD3, which uniquely trains the critic network using hidden states from the actor network as summarized trajectory information. Experimental results in simulation environments demonstrate that including action trajectories improves performance, with H-TD3 showing potential for reduced computational time while maintaining effectiveness.
本文的动机源于强化学习在具有时变扰动和隐藏状态的真实世界应用中面临的挑战，这类问题最适合用部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDPs）来描述。方法上，研究探讨了如何将动作信息与观测一起有效输入循环神经网络（RNN）进行状态估计，并提出了三种新颖的架构算法，其中H-TD3算法独特地利用演员网络生成的隐藏状态作为轨迹摘要信息来训练评论家网络。主要实验结果表明，在仿真环境中，包含动作轨迹能提升算法性能，且H-TD3在保持性能的同时展现了减少计算时间的潜力。
From Heuristic Selection to Automated Algorithm Design: LLMs Benefit from Strong Priors
Authors: Qi Huang, Furong Ye, Ananta Shahane, Thomas Bäck, Niki van Stein
First: 2026-03-03T09:27:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T09:27:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have already been widely adopted for automated algorithm design, demonstrating strong abilities in generating and evolving algorithms across various fields. Existing work has largely focused on examining their effectiveness in solving specific problems, with search strategies primarily guided by adaptive prompt designs. In this paper, through investigating the token-wise attribution of the prompts to LLM-generated algorithmic codes, we show that providing high-quality algorithmic code examples can substantially improve the performance of the LLM-driven optimization. Building upon this insight, we propose leveraging prior benchmark algorithms to guide LLM-driven optimization and demonstrate superior performance on two black-box optimization benchmarks: the pseudo-Boolean optimization suite (pbo) and the black-box optimization suite (bbob). Our findings highlight the value of integrating benchmarking studies to enhance both efficiency and robustness of the LLM-driven black-box optimization methods.

Next Embedding Prediction Makes World Models Stronger
Authors: George Bredis, Nikita Balagansky, Daniil Gavrilov, Ruslan Rakhimov
First: 2026-03-03T09:04:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T09:04:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Capturing temporal dependencies is critical for model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) in partially observable, high-dimensional domains. We introduce NE-Dreamer, a decoder-free MBRL agent that leverages a temporal transformer to predict next-step encoder embeddings from latent state sequences, directly optimizing temporal predictive alignment in representation space. This approach enables NE-Dreamer to learn coherent, predictive state representations without reconstruction losses or auxiliary supervision. On the DeepMind Control Suite, NE-Dreamer matches or exceeds the performance of DreamerV3 and leading decoder-free agents. On a challenging subset of DMLab tasks involving memory and spatial reasoning, NE-Dreamer achieves substantial gains. These results establish next-embedding prediction with temporal transformers as an effective, scalable framework for MBRL in complex, partially observable environments.

Deep learning-guided evolutionary optimization for protein design
Authors: Erik Hartman, Di Tang, Johan Malmström
First: 2026-03-03T08:53:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T08:53:12+00:00
Comments: Code available at GitHub
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Designing novel proteins with desired characteristics remains a significant challenge due to the large sequence space and the complexity of sequence-function relationships. Efficient exploration of this space to identify sequences that meet specific design criteria is crucial for advancing therapeutics and biotechnology. Here, we present BoGA (Bayesian Optimization Genetic Algorithm), a framework that combines evolutionary search with Bayesian optimization to efficiently navigate the sequence space. By integrating a genetic algorithm as a stochastic proposal generator within a surrogate modeling loop, BoGA prioritizes candidates based on prior evaluations and surrogate model predictions, enabling data-efficient optimization. We demonstrate the utility of BoGA through benchmarking on sequence and structure design tasks, followed by its application in designing peptide binders against pneumolysin, a key virulence factor of \textit{Streptococcus pneumoniae}. BoGA accelerates the discovery of high-confidence binders, demonstrating the potential for efficient protein design across diverse objectives. The algorithm is implemented within the BoPep suite and is available under an MIT license at \href{https://github.com/ErikHartman/bopep}{GitHub}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：深度学习引导的进化优化用于蛋白质设计
由于序列空间庞大且序列-功能关系复杂，设计具有所需特性的新型蛋白质仍是一项重大挑战。高效探索该空间以识别符合特定设计标准的序列，对推进治疗学和生物技术发展至关重要。本文提出BoGA（贝叶斯优化遗传算法），该框架将进化搜索与贝叶斯优化相结合，以高效探索序列空间。通过将遗传算法作为随机提案生成器整合至代理模型循环中，BoGA能基于先验评估和代理模型预测对候选序列进行优先级排序，实现数据高效优化。我们通过在序列与结构设计任务上的基准测试，以及针对肺炎链球菌关键毒力因子肺炎溶素设计肽结合剂的应用，展示了BoGA的实用性。BoGA加速了高置信度结合剂的发现，证明了该算法在多样化目标中实现高效蛋白质设计的潜力。该算法已在BoPep套件中实现，并基于MIT许可证发布于GitHub。

Enhancing User Throughput in Multi-panel mmWave Radio Access Networks for Beam-based MU-MIMO Using a DRL Method
Authors: Ramin Hashemi, Vismika Ranasinghe, Teemu Veijalainen, Petteri Kela, Risto Wichman
First: 2026-03-03T08:46:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T08:46:49+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the IEEE International Conference on Communications (ICC) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Millimeter-wave (mmWave) communication systems, particularly those leveraging multi-user multiple-input and multiple-output (MU-MIMO) with hybrid beamforming, face challenges in optimizing user throughput and minimizing latency due to the high complexity of dynamic beam selection and management. This paper introduces a deep reinforcement learning (DRL) approach for enhancing user throughput in multi-panel mmWave radio access networks in a practical network setup. Our DRL-based formulation utilizes an adaptive beam management strategy that models the interaction between the communication agent and its environment as a Markov decision process (MDP), optimizing beam selection based on real-time observations. The proposed framework exploits spatial domain (SD) characteristics by incorporating the cross-correlation between the beams in different antenna panels, the measured reference signal received power (RSRP), and the beam usage statistics to dynamically adjust beamforming decisions. As a result, the spectral efficiency is improved and end-to-end latency is reduced. The numerical results demonstrate an increase in throughput of up to 16% and a reduction in latency by factors 3-7x compared to baseline (legacy beam management).
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的多面板毫米波无线接入网络波束多用户MIMO用户吞吐量增强方法
