Rethinking Policy Diversity in Ensemble Policy Gradient in Large-Scale Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Naoki Shitanda, Motoki Omura, Tatsuya Harada, Takayuki Osa
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T11:06:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T08:32:08+00:00
Comments: In ICLR 2026. Website at https://naoki04.github.io/paper-cpo/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Scaling reinforcement learning to tens of thousands of parallel environments requires overcoming the limited exploration capacity of a single policy. Ensemble-based policy gradient methods, which employ multiple policies to collect diverse samples, have recently been proposed to promote exploration. However, merely broadening the exploration space does not always enhance learning capability, since excessive exploration can reduce exploration quality or compromise training stability. In this work, we theoretically analyze the impact of inter-policy diversity on learning efficiency in policy ensembles, and propose Coupled Policy Optimization which regulates diversity through KL constraints between policies. The proposed method enables effective exploration and outperforms strong baselines such as SAPG, PBT, and PPO across multiple tasks, including challenging dexterous manipulation, in terms of both sample efficiency and final performance. Furthermore, analysis of policy diversity and effective sample size during training reveals that follower policies naturally distribute around the leader, demonstrating the emergence of structured and efficient exploratory behavior. Our results indicate that diverse exploration under appropriate regulation is key to achieving stable and sample-efficient learning in ensemble policy gradient methods. Project page at https://naoki04.github.io/paper-cpo/ .
中文标题/摘要
标题：大规模强化学习中集成策略梯度方法策略多样性的再思考
将强化学习扩展到数万个并行环境需要克服单一策略探索能力有限的问题。近期提出的基于集成的策略梯度方法通过使用多个策略收集多样化样本以促进探索。然而，单纯扩大探索空间并不总能提升学习能力，因为过度探索可能降低探索质量或损害训练稳定性。本文从理论上分析了策略间多样性对集成策略学习效率的影响，并提出通过策略间KL约束调控多样性的耦合策略优化方法。该方法在多个任务（包括具有挑战性的灵巧操作任务）中实现了有效探索，并在样本效率和最终性能上超越了SAPG、PBT、PPO等强基线。训练过程中对策略多样性和有效样本量的分析表明，跟随策略会自然围绕主导策略分布，展现出结构化高效探索行为的涌现。研究结果表明，在适当调控下的多样化探索是实现集成策略梯度方法稳定且样本高效学习的关键。项目页面：https://naoki04.github.io/paper-cpo/
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of limited exploration in large-scale reinforcement learning when scaling to many parallel environments, noting that while ensemble policy gradient methods use multiple policies to increase sample diversity, excessive exploration can harm learning efficiency and stability. To regulate this, the authors propose Coupled Policy Optimization, a method that imposes KL constraints between policies to control inter-policy diversity, theoretically analyzing its impact on learning. Experiments on tasks including dexterous manipulation show that this approach outperforms baselines like SAPG, PBT, and PPO in both sample efficiency and final performance, with analysis revealing that follower policies naturally cluster around a leader, leading to structured and efficient exploratory behavior. The results highlight that properly regulated diversity is crucial for stable and sample-efficient learning in ensemble methods.
本文针对大规模强化学习中扩展到数千并行环境时探索能力有限的问题，指出尽管集成策略梯度方法使用多个策略增加样本多样性，但过度探索可能损害学习效率和稳定性。为此，作者提出了耦合策略优化方法，通过策略间的KL约束来调控多样性，并从理论上分析了其对学习的影响。在包括灵巧操作在内的多个任务上的实验表明，该方法在样本效率和最终性能上均优于SAPG、PBT和PPO等基线，分析显示跟随策略会自然围绕主导策略分布，形成结构化且高效的探索行为。结果表明，适当调控的多样性是实现集成策略梯度方法稳定且样本高效学习的关键。
The Choice of Divergence: A Neglected Key to Mitigating Diversity Collapse in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward
Authors: Long Li, Zhijian Zhou, Jiaran Hao, Jason Klein Liu, Yanting Miao, Wei Pang, Xiaoyu Tan, Wei Chu, Zhe Wang, Shirui Pan, Chao Qu, Yuan Qi
First: 2025-09-09T06:34:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T07:36:26+00:00
Comments: 27 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A central paradox in fine-tuning Large Language Models (LLMs) with Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) is the frequent degradation of multi-attempt performance (Pass@k) despite improvements in single-attempt accuracy (Pass@1). This is often accompanied by catastrophic forgetting, where models lose previously acquired skills. While various methods have been proposed, the choice and function of the divergence term have been surprisingly unexamined as a proactive solution. We argue that standard RLVR objectives -- both those using the mode-seeking reverse KL-divergence and those forgoing a divergence term entirely -- lack a crucial mechanism for knowledge retention. The reverse-KL actively accelerates this decay by narrowing the policy, while its absence provides no safeguard against the model drifting from its diverse knowledge base. We propose a fundamental shift in perspective: using the divergence term itself as the solution. Our framework, Diversity-Preserving Hybrid RL (DPH-RL), leverages mass-covering f-divergences (like forward-KL and JS-divergence) to function as a rehearsal mechanism. By continuously referencing the initial policy, this approach forces the model to maintain broad solution coverage. Extensive experiments on math and SQL generation demonstrate that DPH-RL not only resolves the Pass@k degradation but improves both Pass@1 and Pass@k in- and out-of-domain. Additionally, DPH-RL is more training-efficient because it computes f-divergence using generator functions, requiring only sampling from the initial policy and no online reference model. Our work highlights a crucial, overlooked axis for improving RLVR, demonstrating that the proper selection of a divergence measure is a powerful tool for building more general and diverse reasoning models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：散度选择：强化学习可验证奖励中缓解多样性崩溃的被忽视关键
在使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）微调大型语言模型（LLMs）时，一个核心悖论是：尽管单次尝试准确率（Pass@1）有所提升，但多次尝试性能（Pass@k）却经常下降。这通常伴随着灾难性遗忘，即模型丧失先前习得的技能。尽管已有多种方法被提出，但散度项的选择与功能作为一种主动解决方案却惊人地未被审视。我们认为，标准的RLVR目标——无论是使用寻求模式的反向KL散度还是完全舍弃散度项的方法——都缺乏关键的知识保留机制。反向KL散度通过收窄策略主动加速了这种知识衰减，而舍弃散度项则无法防止模型偏离其多样化的知识基础。我们提出一个根本性的视角转变：将散度项本身作为解决方案。我们的框架——多样性保持混合强化学习（DPH-RL）——利用质量覆盖的f-散度（如正向KL散度和JS散度）作为复现机制。通过持续参考初始策略，该方法迫使模型保持广泛的解决方案覆盖范围。在数学和SQL生成任务上的大量实验表明，DPH-RL不仅解决了Pass@k性能下降问题，还同时提升了领域内外的Pass@1和Pass@k性能。此外，DPH-RL具有更高的训练效率，因为它使用生成函数计算f-散度，仅需从初始策略采样，无需在线参考模型。我们的工作揭示了改进RLVR的一个关键但被忽视的维度，证明正确选择散度度量是构建更通用、更多样化推理模型的强大工具。

This paper addresses the paradox in fine-tuning Large Language Models with Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR), where improvements in single-attempt accuracy (Pass@1) often lead to degraded multi-attempt performance (Pass@k) and catastrophic forgetting. The authors argue that standard RLVR objectives, which use mode-seeking reverse KL-divergence or no divergence term, lack mechanisms for knowledge retention and actively narrow the policy. Shuffle-R1: Efficient RL framework for Multimodal Large Language Models via Data-centric Dynamic Shuffle
Authors: Linghao Zhu, Yiran Guan, Dingkang Liang, Jianzhong Ju, Zhenbo Luo, Bin Qin, Jian Luan, Yuliang Liu, Xiang Bai
Venue: ICLR 2026 poster
First: 2025-08-07T17:53:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T07:07:06+00:00
Comments: This paper has been accepted by ICLR 2026. Conference link: https://iclr.cc/virtual/2026/poster/10007559 OpenReview link: https://openreview.net/forum?id=mYP33u1QBK Project page at: https://xenozlh.github.io/Shuffle-R1/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as an effective post-training paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of multimodal large language model (MLLM). However, current RL pipelines often suffer from training inefficiencies caused by two underexplored issues: Advantage Collapsing, where most advantages in a batch concentrate near zero, and Rollout Silencing, where the proportion of rollouts contributing non-zero gradients diminishes over time. These issues lead to suboptimal gradient updates and hinder long-term learning efficiency. To address these issues, we propose Shuffle-R1, a simple yet principled framework that improves RL fine-tuning efficiency by dynamically restructuring trajectory sampling and batch composition. It introduces (1) Pairwise Trajectory Sampling, which selects high-contrast trajectories with large advantages to improve gradient signal quality, and (2) Advantage-based Trajectory Shuffle, which increases exposure of valuable rollouts through informed batch reshuffling. Experiments across multiple reasoning benchmarks show that our framework consistently outperforms strong RL baselines with minimal overhead. These results highlight the importance of data-centric adaptations for more efficient RL training in MLLM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Shuffle-R1：基于数据动态重排的多模态大语言模型高效强化学习框架
强化学习已成为提升多模态大语言模型推理能力的有效后训练范式。然而，当前强化学习流程常受两个未充分探讨问题导致的训练低效困扰：优势坍缩（批次中多数优势值趋近于零）与轨迹沉寂（贡献非零梯度的轨迹比例随时间递减）。这些问题导致梯度更新次优并阻碍长期学习效率。为解决这些问题，我们提出Shuffle-R1——一个通过动态重组轨迹采样与批次构成来提升强化学习微调效率的简洁而原理清晰的框架。其创新包括：（1）配对轨迹采样：选取具有显著优势差异的高对比度轨迹以提升梯度信号质量；（2）基于优势的轨迹重排：通过智能批次重组增加高价值轨迹的曝光度。在多个推理基准上的实验表明，该框架能以极低开销持续超越主流强化学习基线方法。这些结果凸显了以数据为中心的适应性调整对提升多模态大语言模型强化学习训练效率的重要性。

The proposed Shuffle-R1 framework introduces Pairwise Trajectory Sampling to select high-contrast trajectories and Advantage-based Trajectory Shuffle to reshuffle batches, thereby improving gradient signal quality and rollout exposure. Experimental results across multiple reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that Shuffle-R1 consistently outperforms strong RL baselines with minimal overhead, highlighting the value of data-centric adaptations for efficient RL training.

Improving Diffusion Planners by Self-Supervised Action Gating with Energies
Authors: Yuan Lu, Dongqi Han, Yansen Wang, Dongsheng Li
First: 2026-03-03T06:36:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T06:36:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion planners are a strong approach for offline reinforcement learning, but they can fail when value-guided selection favours trajectories that score well yet are locally inconsistent with the environment dynamics, resulting in brittle execution. We propose Self-supervised Action Gating with Energies (SAGE), an inference-time re-ranking method that penalises dynamically inconsistent plans using a latent consistency signal. SAGE trains a Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) encoder on offline state sequences and an action-conditioned latent predictor for short horizon transitions. At test time, SAGE assigns each sampled candidate an energy given by its latent prediction error and combines this feasibility score with value estimates to select actions. SAGE can integrate into existing diffusion planning pipelines that can sample trajectories and select actions via value scoring; it requires no environment rollouts and no policy re-training. Across locomotion, navigation, and manipulation benchmarks, SAGE improves the performance and robustness of diffusion planners.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过基于能量的自监督动作门控改进扩散规划器
扩散规划器是离线强化学习的有效方法，但当基于价值的选择偏好那些评分高却与环境动态局部不一致的轨迹时，可能导致执行脆弱性。我们提出基于能量的自监督动作门控（SAGE），这是一种推理时重排序方法，通过潜在一致性信号惩罚动态不一致的计划。SAGE在离线状态序列上训练联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）编码器，并构建动作条件潜在预测器用于短时域状态转移。测试时，SAGE根据潜在预测误差为每个采样候选分配能量值，并将此可行性评分与价值估计结合以选择动作。SAGE可集成至现有扩散规划流程（支持轨迹采样和基于价值评分的动作选择），无需环境交互或策略重训练。在运动、导航和操作基准测试中，SAGE显著提升了扩散规划器的性能与鲁棒性。

Experimental results across locomotion, navigation, and manipulation benchmarks demonstrate that SAGE enhances the performance and robustness of diffusion planners without requiring environment rollouts or policy retraining.
本文针对离线强化学习中扩散规划器因价值引导的动作选择可能导致局部不一致轨迹而在执行时失败的问题，提出了一种名为“基于能量的自监督动作门控（SAGE）”的方法。该方法通过在推理时重新排序，利用从离线状态序列和短时程转移训练的联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）中获得的潜在一致性信号，对动态不可行的计划进行惩罚。在运动、导航和操作基准测试中的实验结果表明，SAGE无需环境模拟或策略重新训练，即可显著提升扩散规划器的性能和鲁棒性。
Policy Transfer for Continuous-Time Reinforcement Learning: A (Rough) Differential Equation Approach
Authors: Xin Guo, Zijiu Lyu
First: 2025-10-16T21:57:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T06:17:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper studies policy transfer, one of the well-known transfer learning techniques adopted in large language models, for continuous-time reinforcement learning problems. In the case of continuous-time linear-quadratic systems with Shannon's entropy regularization, we fully exploit the Gaussian structure of their optimal policy and the stability of their associated Riccati equations. In the general case where the system has possibly non-linear and bounded dynamics, the key technical component is the stability of diffusion SDEs which is established by invoking the rough path theory. Our work provides the first theoretical proof of policy transfer for continuous-time RL: an optimal policy learned for one RL problem can be used to initialize to search for a near-optimal policy for another closely related RL problem, while achieving (at least) the same rate of convergence for the original algorithm. As a byproduct of our analysis, we derive the stability of a concrete class of continuous-time score-based diffusion models via their connection with LQRs. To illustrate the benefit of policy transfer for RL, we propose a novel policy learning algorithm for continuous-time LQRs, which achieves global linear convergence and local super-linear convergence.

标题：连续时间强化学习中的策略迁移：一种（粗糙）微分方程方法
本文研究了连续时间强化学习问题中的策略迁移，这是大语言模型所采用的一种著名迁移学习技术。针对具有香农熵正则化的连续时间线性二次系统，我们充分利用了其最优策略的高斯结构及其相关Riccati方程的稳定性。在系统可能具有非线性且有界动力学的一般情况下，关键技术组成部分是扩散随机微分方程的稳定性，这通过调用粗糙路径理论得以建立。我们的工作首次为连续时间强化学习提供了策略迁移的理论证明：针对一个强化学习问题学习到的最优策略，可用于初始化搜索另一个密切相关强化学习问题的近似最优策略，同时（至少）保持原始算法的收敛速度。作为分析的副产品，我们通过其与线性二次调节器的联系，推导了一类具体连续时间基于分数的扩散模型的稳定性。为说明策略迁移对强化学习的益处，我们提出了一种新颖的连续时间线性二次调节器策略学习算法，该算法实现了全局线性收敛和局部超线性收敛。

Quantization-Aware Distillation for NVFP4 Inference Accuracy Recovery
Authors: Meng Xin, Sweta Priyadarshi, Jingyu Xin, Bilal Kartal, Aditya Vavre, Asma Kuriparambil Thekkumpate, Zijia Chen, Ameya Sunil Mahabaleshwarkar, Ido Shahaf, Akhiad Bercovich, Kinjal Patel, Suguna Varshini Velury, Chenjie Luo, Zhiyu Cheng, Jenny Chen, Chen-Han Yu, Wei Ping, Oleg Rybakov, Nima Tajbakhsh, Oluwatobi Olabiyi, Dusan Stosic, Di Wu, Song Han, Eric Chung, Sharath Turuvekere Sreenivas, Bryan Catanzaro, Yoshi Suhara, Tijmen Blankevoort, Huizi Mao
First: 2026-01-27T22:14:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T06:03:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This technical report presents quantization-aware distillation (QAD) and our best practices for recovering accuracy of NVFP4-quantized large language models (LLMs) and vision-language models (VLMs). QAD distills a full-precision teacher model into a quantized student model using a KL divergence loss. While applying distillation to quantized models is not a new idea, we observe key advantages of QAD for today's LLMs: 1. It shows remarkable effectiveness and stability for models trained through multi-stage post-training pipelines, including supervised fine-tuning (SFT), reinforcement learning (RL), and model merging, where traditional quantization-aware training (QAT) suffers from engineering complexity and training instability; 2. It is robust to data quality and coverage, enabling accuracy recovery without full training data. We evaluate QAD across multiple post-trained models including AceReason Nemotron, Nemotron 3 Nano, Nemotron Nano V2, Nemotron Nano V2 VL (VLM), and Llama Nemotron Super v1, showing consistent recovery to near-BF16 accuracy.

Post Hoc Extraction of Pareto Fronts for Continuous Control
Authors: Raghav Thakar, Gaurav Dixit, Kagan Tumer
Venue: IJCAI 2026
First: 2026-03-03T05:57:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T05:57:59+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 4 figures. Submitted to IJCAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agents in the real world must often balance multiple objectives, such as speed, stability, and energy efficiency in continuous control. To account for changing conditions and preferences, an agent must ideally learn a Pareto frontier of policies representing multiple optimal trade-offs. Recent advances in multi-policy multi-objective reinforcement learning (MORL) enable learning a Pareto front directly, but require full multi-objective consideration from the start of training. In practice, multi-objective preferences often arise after a policy has already been trained on a single specialised objective. Existing MORL methods cannot leverage these pre-trained `specialists' to learn Pareto fronts and avoid incurring the sample costs of retraining. We introduce Mixed Advantage Pareto Extraction (MAPEX), an offline MORL method that constructs a frontier of policies by reusing pre-trained specialist policies, critics, and replay buffers. MAPEX combines evaluations from specialist critics into a mixed advantage signal, and weights a behaviour cloning loss with it to train new policies that balance multiple objectives. MAPEX's post hoc Pareto front extraction preserves the simplicity of single-objective off-policy RL, and avoids retrofitting these algorithms into complex MORL frameworks. We formally describe the MAPEX procedure and evaluate MAPEX on five multi-objective MuJoCo environments. Given the same starting policies, MAPEX produces comparable fronts at $0.001\%$ the sample cost of established baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续控制中帕累托前沿的后验提取方法
现实世界中的智能体常需平衡多个目标，如连续控制中的速度、稳定性和能效。为适应动态环境与偏好变化，理想情况下智能体应学习表征多目标最优权衡的帕累托前沿策略集。虽然近期多策略多目标强化学习（MORL）的进展能直接学习帕累托前沿，但需从训练初始就进行完整多目标考量。实践中，多目标偏好往往在单目标专家策略训练完成后才出现。现有MORL方法无法利用这些预训练的‘专家策略’来构建帕累托前沿，且难以避免重新训练的高样本成本。本文提出混合优势帕累托提取（MAPEX）——一种离线MORL方法，通过复用预训练的专家策略、评论家网络和回放缓冲区来构建策略前沿。MAPEX将专家评论家的评估结果融合为混合优势信号，并以此加权行为克隆损失来训练平衡多目标的新策略。该方法的后验帕累托前沿提取保持了单目标离线策略强化学习的简洁性，无需将算法改造为复杂MORL框架。我们形式化描述了MAPEX流程，并在五个多目标MuJoCo环境中进行评估。在相同初始策略条件下，MAPEX能以基线方法0.001%的样本成本生成可比拟的帕累托前沿。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that real-world agents must balance multiple objectives, but multi-objective reinforcement learning (MORL) typically requires expensive training from scratch, even when pre-trained specialist policies for single objectives already exist. The method introduced, called Mixed Advantage Pareto Extraction (MAPEX), is an offline MORL approach that extracts a Pareto frontier by reusing pre-trained specialists, their critics, and replay buffers; it combines critic evaluations into a mixed advantage signal to weight a behavior cloning loss for training new, balanced policies. The main experimental results, from evaluations on five multi-objective MuJoCo environments, show that MAPEX can produce comparable Pareto fronts to established baselines while using only 0.001% of the sample cost, given the same starting specialist policies.

Real-Time Generative Policy via Langevin-Guided Flow Matching for Autonomous Driving
Authors: Tianze Zhu, Yinuo Wang, Wenjun Zou, Tianyi Zhang, Likun Wang, Letian Tao, Feihong Zhang, Yao Lyu, Shengbo Eben Li
First: 2026-03-03T05:35:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T05:35:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) is a fundamental methodology in autonomous driving systems, where generative policies exhibit considerable potential by leveraging their ability to model complex distributions to enhance exploration. However, their inherent high inference latency severely impedes their deployment in real-time decision-making and control. To address this issue, we propose diffusion actor-critic with entropy regulator via flow matching (DACER-F) by introducing flow matching into online RL, enabling the generation of competitive actions in a single inference step. By leveraging Langevin dynamics and gradients of the Q-function, DACER-F dynamically optimizes actions from experience replay toward a target distribution that balances high Q-value information with exploratory behavior. The flow policy is then trained to efficiently learn a mapping from a simple prior distribution to this dynamic target. In complex multi-lane and intersection simulations, DACER-F outperforms baselines diffusion actor-critic with entropy regulator (DACER) and distributional soft actor-critic (DSAC), while maintaining an ultra-low inference latency. DACER-F further demonstrates its scalability on standard RL benchmark DeepMind Control Suite (DMC), achieving a score of 775.8 in the humanoid-stand task and surpassing prior methods. Collectively, these results establish DACER-F as a high-performance and computationally efficient RL algorithm.

Heterogeneous Agent Collaborative Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhixia Zhang, Zixuan Huang, Xin Xia, Deqing Wang, Fuzhen Zhuang, Shuai Ma, Ning Ding, Yaodong Yang, Jianxin Li, Yikun Ban
First: 2026-03-03T05:09:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T05:09:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Heterogeneous Agent Collaborative Reinforcement Learning (HACRL), a new learning paradigm that addresses the inefficiencies of isolated on-policy optimization. HACRL enables collaborative optimization with independent execution: heterogeneous agents share verified rollouts during training to mutually improve, while operating independently at inference time. Unlike LLM-based multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), HACRL does not require coordinated deployment, and unlike on-/off-policy distillation, it enables bidirectional mutual learning among heterogeneous agents rather than one-directional teacher-to-student transfer. Building on this paradigm, we propose HACPO, a collaborative RL algorithm that enables principled rollout sharing to maximize sample utilization and cross-agent knowledge transfer. To mitigate capability discrepancies and policy distribution shifts, HACPO introduces four tailored mechanisms with theoretical guarantees on unbiased advantage estimation and optimization correctness. Extensive experiments across diverse heterogeneous model combinations and reasoning benchmarks show that HACPO consistently improves all participating agents, outperforming GSPO by an average of 3.3\% while using only half the rollout cost.

Motivated by the inefficiencies of isolated on-policy optimization, this paper introduces Heterogeneous Agent Collaborative Reinforcement Learning (HACRL), a paradigm enabling agents to share verified rollouts during training for mutual improvement while maintaining independent execution at inference. The method is instantiated as HACPO, an algorithm that facilitates principled rollout sharing with mechanisms to address capability discrepancies and policy shifts, backed by theoretical guarantees. Non-Rectangular Average-Reward Robust MDPs: Optimal Policies and Their Transient Values
Authors: Shengbo Wang, Nian Si
First: 2026-03-01T06:29:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T04:40:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study non-rectangular robust Markov decision processes under the average-reward criterion, where the ambiguity set couples transition probabilities across states and the adversary commits to a stationary kernel for the entire horizon. We show that any history-dependent policy achieving sublinear expected regret uniformly over the ambiguity set is robust-optimal, and that the robust value admits a minimax representation as the infimum over the ambiguity set of the classical optimal gains, without requiring any form of rectangularity or robust dynamic programming principle. Under the weak communication assumption, we establish the existence of such policies by converting high-probability regret bounds from the average-reward reinforcement learning literature into the expected-regret criterion. We then introduce a transient-value framework to evaluate finite-time performance of robust optimal policies, proving that average-reward optimality alone can mask arbitrarily poor transients and deriving regret-based lower bounds on transient values. Finally, we construct an epoch-based policy that combines an optimal stationary policy for the worst-case model with an anytime-valid sequential test and an online learning fallback, achieving a constant-order transient value.
中文标题/摘要
标题：非矩形平均奖励鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程：最优策略及其瞬态值
我们研究了平均奖励准则下的非矩形鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程，其中模糊集耦合了状态间的转移概率，且对手在整个时间范围内承诺使用固定核。我们证明，任何在模糊集上一致实现次线性期望遗憾的历史依赖策略都是鲁棒最优的，且鲁棒值可表示为经典最优增益在模糊集上的极小极大表示，无需任何形式的矩形性或鲁棒动态规划原理。在弱通信假设下，通过将平均奖励强化学习文献中的高概率遗憾界转化为期望遗憾准则，我们证明了此类策略的存在性。随后，我们引入瞬态值框架来评估鲁棒最优策略的有限时间性能，证明仅凭平均奖励最优性可能掩盖任意差的瞬态表现，并基于遗憾推导瞬态值的下界。最后，我们构建了一种基于周期的策略，该策略结合了最坏情况模型的最优固定策略、任意时间有效的序贯检验以及在线学习回退机制，实现了常数阶的瞬态值。

MedXIAOHE: A Comprehensive Recipe for Building Medical MLLMs
Authors: Baorong Shi, Bo Cui, Boyuan Jiang, Deli Yu, Fang Qian, Haihua Yang, Huichao Wang, Jiale Chen, Jianfei Pan, Jieqiong Cao, Jinghao Lin, Kai Wu, Lin Yang, Shengsheng Yao, Tao Chen, Xiaojun Xiao, Xiaozhong Ji, Xu Wang, Yijun He, Zhixiong Yang

Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present MedXIAOHE, a medical vision-language foundation model designed to advance general-purpose medical understanding and reasoning in real-world clinical applications. MedXIAOHE achieves state-of-the-art performance across diverse medical benchmarks and surpasses leading closed-source multimodal systems on multiple capabilities. To achieve this, we propose an entity-aware continual pretraining framework that organizes heterogeneous medical corpora to broaden knowledge coverage and reduce long-tail gaps (e.g., rare diseases). For medical expert-level reasoning and interaction, MedXIAOHE incorporates diverse medical reasoning patterns via reinforcement learning and tool-augmented agentic training, enabling multi-step diagnostic reasoning with verifiable decision traces. To improve reliability in real-world use, MedXIAOHE integrates user-preference rubrics, evidence-grounded reasoning, and low-hallucination long-form report generation, with improved adherence to medical instructions. We release this report to document our practical design choices, scaling insights, and evaluation framework, hoping to inspire further research.

Towards Parameter-Free Temporal Difference Learning
Authors: Yunxiang Li, Mark Schmidt, Reza Babanezhad, Sharan Vaswani
First: 2026-03-03T03:49:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T03:49:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Temporal difference (TD) learning is a fundamental algorithm for estimating value functions in reinforcement learning. Recent finite-time analyses of TD with linear function approximation quantify its theoretical convergence rate. However, they often require setting the algorithm parameters using problem-dependent quantities that are difficult to estimate in practice -- such as the minimum eigenvalue of the feature covariance (\(ω\)) or the mixing time of the underlying Markov chain (\(τ_{\text{mix}}\)). In addition, some analyses rely on nonstandard and impractical modifications, exacerbating the gap between theory and practice. To address these limitations, we use an exponential step-size schedule with the standard TD(0) algorithm. We analyze the resulting method under two sampling regimes: independent and identically distributed (i.i.d.) sampling from the stationary distribution, and the more practical Markovian sampling along a single trajectory. In the i.i.d.\ setting, the proposed algorithm does not require knowledge of problem-dependent quantities such as \(ω\), and attains the optimal bias-variance trade-off for the last iterate. In the Markovian setting, we propose a regularized TD(0) algorithm with an exponential step-size schedule. The resulting algorithm achieves a comparable convergence rate to prior works, without requiring projections, iterate averaging, or knowledge of \(τ_{\text{mix}}\) or \(ω\).
中文标题/摘要
标题：迈向无参数时序差分学习
时序差分（TD）学习是强化学习中估计价值函数的基础算法。近期针对线性函数逼近下TD的有限时间分析量化了其理论收敛速率，但这些分析通常需要根据问题相关的量（如特征协方差的最小特征值（ω）或底层马尔可夫链的混合时间（τ_mix））来设置算法参数，而这些量在实践中难以估计。此外，部分分析依赖非标准且不实用的修改，加剧了理论与实践的脱节。为解决这些局限，我们在标准TD(0)算法中引入指数步长调度。我们在两种采样机制下分析所得方法：从平稳分布中独立同分布（i.i.d.）采样，以及更实用的沿单条轨迹的马尔可夫采样。在i.i.d.设置中，所提算法无需知晓ω等问题相关量，并对最终迭代实现了最优偏差-方差权衡。在马尔可夫设置中，我们提出采用指数步长调度的正则化TD(0)算法，该算法在不需投影、迭代平均或知晓τ_mix与ω的情况下，达到了与先前工作相当的收敛速率。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the practical limitations of temporal difference (TD) learning, where existing finite-time convergence analyses often depend on hard-to-estimate problem parameters like the minimum eigenvalue of the feature covariance or the Markov chain mixing time, and sometimes require nonstandard algorithmic modifications. To bridge this theory-practice gap, the authors propose using an exponential step-size schedule with standard TD(0) and, for Markovian sampling, a regularized variant. Their main experimental results show that under independent sampling, the method achieves an optimal bias-variance trade-off for the last iterate without prior knowledge of problem parameters, and under Markovian sampling, it attains a comparable convergence rate without needing projections, iterate averaging, or estimates of the mixing time or eigenvalue.
本文针对时序差分学习中的实践局限性提出改进，现有有限时间收敛分析通常依赖于难以估计的问题参数，如特征协方差的最小特征值或马尔可夫链的混合时间，且有时需要非标准的算法修改。为弥合理论与实践的差距，作者提出在标准TD(0)中使用指数步长调度，并对马尔可夫采样采用正则化变体。主要实验结果表明，在独立采样下，该方法无需先验知识即可实现最终迭代的最优偏差-方差权衡；在马尔可夫采样下，无需投影、迭代平均或对混合时间与特征值的估计，即可达到与先前工作相当的收敛速率。
Wasserstein Proximal Policy Gradient
Authors: Zhaoyu Zhu, Shuhan Zhang, Rui Gao, Shuang Li
First: 2026-03-03T03:48:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T03:48:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study policy gradient methods for continuous-action, entropy-regularized reinforcement learning through the lens of Wasserstein geometry. Starting from a Wasserstein proximal update, we derive Wasserstein Proximal Policy Gradient (WPPG) via an operator-splitting scheme that alternates an optimal transport update with a heat step implemented by Gaussian convolution. This formulation avoids evaluating the policy's log density or its gradient, making the method directly applicable to expressive implicit stochastic policies specified as pushforward maps. We establish a global linear convergence rate for WPPG, covering both exact policy evaluation and actor-critic implementations with controlled approximation error. Empirically, WPPG is simple to implement and attains competitive performance on standard continuous-control benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Wasserstein近端策略梯度
本研究从Wasserstein几何视角出发，探讨连续动作熵正则化强化学习的策略梯度方法。基于Wasserstein近端更新，我们通过算子分裂方案推导出Wasserstein近端策略梯度（WPPG），该方案交替执行最优传输更新与通过高斯卷积实现的热扩散步骤。该公式避免评估策略的对数密度或其梯度，使方法可直接适用于由前推映射定义的表达性隐式随机策略。我们建立了WPPG的全局线性收敛速率，涵盖精确策略评估与具有受控近似误差的执行者-评论者实现。实证表明，WPPG易于实现，并在标准连续控制基准测试中取得具有竞争力的性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Wasserstein Proximal Policy Gradient (WPPG), motivated by leveraging Wasserstein geometry to enhance policy gradient methods for continuous-action reinforcement learning with entropy regularization. The method derives from a Wasserstein proximal update, using an operator-splitting scheme that alternates between an optimal transport step and a Gaussian convolution heat step, which avoids computing the policy's log density or gradient and supports implicit stochastic policies defined as pushforward maps. Experimental results demonstrate that WPPG achieves global linear convergence theoretically and delivers competitive performance on standard continuous-control benchmarks, while being straightforward to implement.
本文提出了Wasserstein近端策略梯度（WPPG），其动机是利用Wasserstein几何改进连续动作、熵正则化强化学习中的策略梯度方法。该方法基于Wasserstein近端更新，通过算子分裂方案交替进行最优传输步骤和高斯卷积热步骤，避免了计算策略的对数密度或梯度，并支持定义为前推映射的隐式随机策略。实验结果表明，WPPG在理论上实现了全局线性收敛，并在标准连续控制基准测试中取得了有竞争力的性能，同时易于实现。
Combinatorial Rising Bandits
Authors: Seockbean Song, Youngsik Yoon, Siwei Wang, Wei Chen, Jungseul Ok
First: 2024-12-01T12:52:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T03:42:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Combinatorial online learning is a fundamental task for selecting the optimal action (or super arm) as a combination of base arms in sequential interactions with systems providing stochastic rewards. It is applicable to diverse domains such as robotics, social advertising, network routing, and recommendation systems. In many real-world scenarios, we often encounter rising rewards, where playing a base arm not only provides an instantaneous reward but also contributes to the enhancement of future rewards, e.g., robots improving through practice and social influence strengthening in the history of successful recommendations. Crucially, these enhancements may propagate to multiple super arms that share the same base arms, introducing dependencies beyond the scope of existing bandit models. To address this gap, we introduce the Combinatorial Rising Bandit (CRB) framework and propose a provably efficient and empirically effective algorithm, Combinatorial Rising Upper Confidence Bound (CRUCB). We empirically demonstrate the effectiveness of CRUCB in realistic deep reinforcement learning environments and synthetic settings, while our theoretical analysis establishes tight regret bounds. Together, they underscore the practical impact and theoretical rigor of our approach. Our code is available at https://github.com/ml-postech/Combinatorial-Rising-Bandits.
中文标题/摘要
标题：组合式上升赌博机
组合在线学习是一种基础任务，旨在通过与提供随机奖励的系统进行序贯交互，选择作为基础臂组合的最优动作（或超级臂）。该任务适用于机器人学、社交广告、网络路由和推荐系统等多个领域。在许多现实场景中，我们常遇到奖励上升现象：拉动一个基础臂不仅提供即时奖励，还能增强未来奖励，例如机器人通过练习提升能力，或成功推荐历史中社交影响力的强化。关键在于，这些增强效应可能传播到共享相同基础臂的多个超级臂，从而引入了现有赌博机模型无法涵盖的依赖关系。为填补这一空白，我们提出了组合式上升赌博机（CRB）框架，并设计了一种理论高效且实证有效的算法——组合式上升置信上界（CRUCB）。我们在真实深度强化学习环境和合成设置中实证验证了CRUCB的有效性，同时理论分析确立了严格的遗憾界。两者共同凸显了本方法的实际影响与理论严谨性。代码发布于 https://github.com/ml-postech/Combinatorial-Rising-Bandits。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces the Combinatorial Rising Bandit (CRB) framework to address combinatorial online learning problems where base arms exhibit rising rewards—meaning each play not only yields an immediate reward but also enhances future rewards for all super arms sharing that base arm, a dependency not captured by existing bandit models. The authors propose the Combinatorial Rising Upper Confidence Bound (CRUCB) algorithm, which is designed to efficiently handle these dependencies. Experimental results in both synthetic settings and realistic deep reinforcement learning environments demonstrate the algorithm's effectiveness, while theoretical analysis provides tight regret bounds, confirming both practical utility and theoretical soundness.
本文提出了组合上升赌博机（CRB）框架，以解决组合在线学习问题，其中基础臂具有上升奖励特性——即每次拉动不仅产生即时奖励，还会提升所有共享该基础臂的超臂的未来奖励，这种依赖关系是现有赌博机模型未能涵盖的。作者设计了组合上升置信上界（CRUCB）算法，以高效处理这些依赖关系。在合成环境和现实的深度强化学习场景中的实验结果表明了该算法的有效性，同时理论分析给出了紧密的遗憾界，验证了方法的实用性和理论严谨性。
Perception-R1: Advancing Multimodal Reasoning Capabilities of MLLMs via Visual Perception Reward
Authors: Tong Xiao, Xin Xu, Zhenya Huang, Hongyu Gao, Quan Liu, Qi Liu, Enhong Chen
First: 2025-06-08T16:48:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T03:04:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Enhancing the multimodal reasoning capabilities of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) is a challenging task that has attracted increasing attention in the community. Recently, several studies have applied Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) to the multimodal domain in order to enhance the reasoning abilities of MLLMs. However, these works largely overlook the enhancement of multimodal perception capabilities in MLLMs, which serve as a core prerequisite and foundational component of complex multimodal reasoning. Through McNemar's test, we find that existing RLVR method fails to effectively enhance the multimodal perception capabilities of MLLMs, thereby limiting their further improvement in multimodal reasoning. To address this limitation, we propose Perception-R1, which introduces a novel visual perception reward that explicitly encourages MLLMs to perceive the visual content accurately, thereby can effectively incentivizing both their multimodal perception and reasoning capabilities. Specifically, we first collect textual visual annotations from the CoT trajectories of multimodal problems, which will serve as visual references for reward assignment. During RLVR training, we employ a judging LLM to assess the consistency between the visual annotations and the responses generated by MLLM, and assign the visual perception reward based on these consistency judgments. Extensive experiments on several multimodal reasoning benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of our Perception-R1, which achieves state-of-the-art performance on most benchmarks using only 1,442 training data. Our code and dataset will be available at https://github.com/tongxiao2002/Perception-R1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Perception-R1：通过视觉感知奖励提升多模态大语言模型的多模态推理能力
增强多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的多模态推理能力是一项具有挑战性的任务，已引起学界日益关注。近期，多项研究将可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）应用于多模态领域，以提升MLLMs的推理能力。然而，这些工作大多忽视了MLLMs多模态感知能力的增强，而该能力是复杂多模态推理的核心前提与基础组成部分。通过麦克尼马尔检验，我们发现现有RLVR方法未能有效提升MLLMs的多模态感知能力，从而限制了其在多模态推理方面的进一步改进。为突破此局限，我们提出Perception-R1，引入一种新颖的视觉感知奖励机制，明确激励MLLMs准确感知视觉内容，从而有效提升其多模态感知与推理能力。具体而言，我们首先从多模态问题的思维链轨迹中收集文本化视觉标注，作为奖励分配的视觉参照。在RLVR训练过程中，采用评判大语言模型评估视觉标注与MLLM生成回答的一致性，并基于一致性判断分配视觉感知奖励。在多个多模态推理基准上的大量实验证明了Perception-R1的有效性，仅使用1,442条训练数据即在多数基准上达到最先进性能。代码与数据集发布于https://github.com/tongxiao2002/Perception-R1。

The proposed method, Perception-R1, introduces a novel visual perception reward that explicitly encourages accurate visual content perception by using textual visual annotations from Chain-of-Thought trajectories as references and employing a judging LLM to assess consistency between these annotations and MLLM responses during training. Network Topology Optimization via Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhuoran Li, Xing Wang, Ling Pan, Lin Zhu, Zhendong Wang, Junlan Feng, Chao Deng, Longbo Huang
First: 2022-04-19T07:45:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T02:59:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Topology impacts important network performance metrics, including link utilization, throughput and latency, and is of central importance to network operators. However, due to the combinatorial nature of network topology, it is extremely difficult to obtain an optimal solution, especially since topology planning in networks also often comes with management-specific constraints. As a result, local optimization with hand-tuned heuristic methods from human experts is often adopted in practice. Yet, heuristic methods cannot cover the global topology design space while taking into account constraints, and cannot guarantee to find good solutions. In this paper, we propose a novel deep reinforcement learning (DRL) algorithm for graph searching, called DRL-GS, for network topology optimization. DRL-GS consists of three novel components, including a verifier to validate the correctness of a generated network topology, a graph neural network (GNN) to efficiently approximate topology rating, and a DRL agent to conduct a topology search. DRL-GS can efficiently search over relatively large topology space and output topology with satisfactory performance. We conduct a case study based on a real-world network scenario, and our experimental results demonstrate the superior performance of DRL-GS in terms of both efficiency and performance.

Beyond State-Wise Mirror Descent: Offline Policy Optimization with Parameteric Policies
Authors: Xiang Li, Yuheng Zhang, Nan Jiang
First: 2026-02-27T08:51:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T02:13:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We investigate the theoretical aspects of offline reinforcement learning (RL) under general function approximation. While prior works (e.g., Xie et al., 2021) have established the theoretical foundations of learning a good policy from offline data via pessimism, existing algorithms that are computationally tractable (often in an oracle-efficient sense), such as PSPI, only apply to finite and small action spaces. Moreover, these algorithms rely on state-wise mirror descent and require actors to be implicitly induced from the critic functions, failing to accommodate standalone policy parameterization which is ubiquitous in practice. In this work, we address these limitations and extend the theoretical guarantees to parameterized policy classes over large or continuous action spaces. When extending mirror descent to parameterized policies, we identify contextual coupling as the core difficulty, and show how connecting mirror descent to natural policy gradient leads to novel analyses, guarantees, and algorithmic insights, including a surprising unification between offline RL and imitation learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越状态级镜像下降：基于参数化策略的离线策略优化
本文研究了一般函数逼近下离线强化学习的理论问题。尽管先前研究（如Xie等人，2021）已通过悲观主义方法建立了从离线数据学习优质策略的理论基础，但现有计算可行的算法（通常具有预言机效率），如PSPI，仅适用于有限的小动作空间。此外，这些算法依赖状态级镜像下降，要求从评价函数隐式推导执行者，无法适应实践中普遍存在的独立策略参数化。本研究针对这些局限，将理论保证扩展至大动作空间或连续动作空间的参数化策略类。在将镜像下降推广至参数化策略时，我们指出上下文耦合是核心难点，并通过将镜像下降与自然策略梯度相关联，提出了新的分析框架、理论保证和算法洞见，包括离线强化学习与模仿学习之间令人惊异的统一性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitations of existing offline reinforcement learning methods, which are computationally tractable only for small discrete action spaces and rely on state-wise mirror descent that cannot accommodate standalone parametric policies. The authors propose extending mirror descent to parameterized policy classes over large or continuous action spaces by identifying and overcoming the challenge of contextual coupling, connecting mirror descent to natural policy gradient to enable novel analyses and algorithmic insights. Their theoretical contributions show that this approach unifies offline RL with imitation learning, providing guarantees for learning good policies from offline data under general function approximation.
本文针对现有离线强化学习方法的局限性展开研究，这些方法仅适用于小型离散动作空间且依赖于状态镜像下降法，无法兼容实践中普遍使用的独立参数化策略。作者通过将镜像下降法扩展到大型或连续动作空间的参数化策略类，识别并克服了上下文耦合这一核心难点，将镜像下降与自然策略梯度联系起来，从而实现了新的理论分析和算法见解。研究结果表明，该方法统一了离线强化学习与模仿学习，为在一般函数逼近下从离线数据中学习优质策略提供了理论保证。
Optimizing Orbital Parameters of Satellites for a Global Quantum Network
Authors: Athul Ashok, Owen DePoint, Jackson MacDonald, Albert Williams, Don Towsley
First: 2026-03-03T00:08:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T00:08:52+00:00
Comments: Long (8 page, 5 figure) version of paper appearing at QCNC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Due to fundamental limitations on terrestrial quantum links, satellites have received considerable attention for their potential as entanglement generation sources in a global quantum internet. In this work, we focus on the problem of designing a constellation of satellites for such a quantum network. We find satellite inclination angles and satellite cluster allocations to achieve maximal entanglement generation rates to fixed sets of globally distributed ground stations. Exploring two black-box optimization frameworks: a Bayesian Optimization (BO) approach and a Genetic Algorithm (GA) approach, we find comparable results, indicating their effectiveness for this optimization task. While GA and BO often perform remarkably similar, BO often converges more efficiently, while later growth noted in GAs is indicative of less susceptibility towards local maxima. In either case, they offer substantial improvements over naive approaches that maximize coverage with respect to ground station placement.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向全球量子网络的卫星轨道参数优化
由于地面量子链路存在根本性限制，卫星作为全球量子互联网中纠缠态生成源的潜力备受关注。本研究聚焦于为量子网络设计卫星星座的问题，通过优化卫星倾角与集群分配，实现面向全球固定地面站的最大纠缠态生成速率。探索了两种黑盒优化框架：贝叶斯优化（BO）与遗传算法（GA），两者结果相当，均证明对此优化任务有效。GA与BO表现常高度相似，但BO收敛更高效，而GA后期增长趋势显示其更不易陷入局部最优。两种方法相较仅依据地面站位置最大化覆盖的朴素方案均有显著提升。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of terrestrial quantum links by designing satellite constellations for a global quantum internet, aiming to maximize entanglement generation rates with ground stations. CORE: Concept-Oriented Reinforcement for Bridging the Definition-Application Gap in Mathematical Reasoning
Authors: Zijun Gao, Zhikun Xu, Xiao Ye, Ben Zhou
First: 2025-12-21T19:01:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T21:29:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) often solve challenging math exercises yet fail to apply the concept right when the problem requires genuine understanding. Popular Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) pipelines reinforce final answers but provide little fine-grained conceptual signal, so models improve at pattern reuse rather than conceptual applications. We introduce CORE (Concept-Oriented REinforcement), an RL training framework that turns explicit concepts into a controllable supervision signal. Starting from a high-quality, low-contamination textbook resource that links verifiable exercises to concise concept descriptions, we run a sanity probe showing LLMs can restate definitions but fail concept-linked quizzes, quantifying the conceptual reasoning gap. CORE then (i) synthesizes concept-aligned quizzes, (ii) injects brief concept snippets during rollouts to elicit concept-primed trajectories, and (iii) reinforces conceptual reasoning via trajectory replacement after group failures, a lightweight forward-KL constraint that aligns unguided with concept-primed policies, or standard GRPO directly on concept-aligned quizzes. Across several models, CORE delivers consistent gains over vanilla and SFT baselines on both in-domain concept-exercise suites and diverse out-of-domain math benchmarks. CORE unifies direct training on concept-aligned quizzes and concept-injected rollouts under outcome regularization. It provides fine-grained conceptual supervision that bridges problem-solving competence and genuine conceptual reasoning, while remaining algorithm- and verifier-agnostic.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CORE：面向概念的强化学习——弥合数学推理中定义与应用间的鸿沟
大语言模型（LLMs）常能解决复杂数学题，却在需要真正理解概念的应用场景中失效。主流“可验证奖励的强化学习”（RLVR）流程虽能强化最终答案，却缺乏细粒度的概念信号，导致模型仅提升模式复用能力而非概念应用能力。本文提出CORE（面向概念的强化学习），一种将显式概念转化为可控监督信号的RL训练框架。基于高质量、低噪声的教材资源（其将可验证习题与精确定义的概念描述关联），我们通过诊断实验发现：LLMs能复述定义，却在概念关联测验中失败，量化了概念推理的差距。CORE随后（i）合成概念对齐的测验，（ii）在策略推演中注入简短概念片段以激发概念引导的轨迹，（iii）通过组失败后的轨迹替换强化概念推理——采用轻量级前向KL约束对齐无引导与概念引导策略，或直接在概念对齐测验上应用标准GRPO。在多模型实验中，CORE在领域内概念习题集与多样化的领域外数学基准上，均较原始基线及监督微调基线取得稳定提升。CORE通过结果正则化，将概念对齐测验的直接训练与概念注入式推演相统一，提供了细粒度的概念监督，弥合解题能力与真实概念推理间的鸿沟，且保持算法与验证器的无关性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue that large language models (LLMs) often solve math exercises through pattern reuse rather than genuine conceptual understanding, creating a gap between knowing definitions and applying concepts. To bridge this, the authors propose CORE (Concept-Oriented REinforcement), a reinforcement learning framework that uses explicit concepts as supervision by synthesizing concept-aligned quizzes, injecting concept snippets during rollouts to guide reasoning, and reinforcing conceptual trajectories via methods like trajectory replacement or GRPO. Experimental results show that CORE consistently improves performance over baselines on both in-domain concept exercises and out-of-domain math benchmarks, effectively enhancing conceptual reasoning without relying on specific algorithms or verifiers.
本文针对大语言模型在数学推理中常通过模式复用解题而非真正理解概念，导致定义与应用之间存在差距的问题，提出了CORE（概念导向强化学习）框架。该方法将明确的概念转化为监督信号，通过合成概念对齐的测验、在推理过程中注入概念提示以引导轨迹，并采用轨迹替换或GRPO等技术强化概念推理。实验结果表明，CORE在领域内的概念练习和领域外的数学基准测试上均优于基线和微调方法，有效提升了模型的概念理解能力，且不依赖于特定算法或验证器。
COOL-MC: Verifying and Explaining RL Policies for Platelet Inventory Management
Authors: Dennis Gross
First: 2026-03-02T21:17:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T21:17:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Platelets expire within five days. Blood banks face uncertain daily demand and must balance ordering decisions between costly wastage from overstocking and life-threatening shortages from understocking. Reinforcement learning (RL) can learn effective ordering policies for this Markov decision process (MDP), but the resulting neural policies remain black boxes, hindering trust and adoption in safety-critical domains. We apply COOL-MC, a tool that combines RL with probabilistic model checking and explainable RL, to verify and explain a trained policy for the MDP on platelet inventory management inspired by Haijema et al. By constructing a policy-induced discrete-time Markov chain (which includes only the reachable states under the trained policy to reduce memory usage), we verify PCTL properties and provide feature-level explanations. Results show that the trained policy achieves a 2.9% stockout probability and a 1.1% inventory-full (potential wastage) probability within a 200-step horizon, primarily attends to the age distribution of inventory rather than other features such as day of week or pending orders. Action reachability analysis reveals that the policy employs a diverse replenishment strategy, with most order quantities reached quickly, while several are never selected. Counterfactual analysis shows that replacing medium-large orders with smaller ones leaves both safety probabilities nearly unchanged, indicating that these orders are placed in well-buffered inventory states. This first formal verification and explanation of an RL platelet inventory management policy demonstrates COOL-MC's value for transparent, auditable decision-making in safety-critical healthcare supply chain domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：COOL-MC：血小板库存管理强化学习策略的形式化验证与解释
血小板保质期仅五天。血库面临不确定的日需求量，必须在过量订购导致的高成本浪费与库存不足引发的生命威胁之间取得平衡。强化学习（RL）可为该马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）学习有效的订购策略，但生成的神经网络策略仍是黑箱，阻碍了其在安全关键领域的可信度与应用。本研究应用COOL-MC工具（融合强化学习、概率模型检验与可解释强化学习），对受Haijema等人启发的血小板库存管理MDP训练策略进行验证与解释。通过构建策略诱导的离散时间马尔可夫链（仅包含训练策略可达状态以降低内存占用），我们验证了PCTL属性并提供特征级解释。结果表明：在200步时限内，训练策略实现2.9%的缺货概率与1.1%的满库（潜在浪费）概率；策略主要关注库存年龄分布，而非星期几或待处理订单等特征。动作可达性分析显示策略采用多样化补货方案，多数订单量可快速达成，但部分订单量从未被选择。反事实分析表明，将中大订单替换为小订单时安全概率几乎不变，说明这些订单仅在库存缓冲充足时执行。此项首次对RL血小板库存管理策略的形式化验证与解释，证明了COOL-MC在安全关键医疗供应链领域实现透明、可审计决策的价值。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for trustworthy and transparent decision-making in safety-critical healthcare supply chains, this paper applies the COOL-MC tool to verify and explain a reinforcement learning (RL) policy for platelet inventory management, where balancing wastage and shortages is critical. The method integrates RL with probabilistic model checking and explainable AI by constructing a policy-induced Markov chain to verify probabilistic computational tree logic (PCTL) properties and generate feature-level explanations. Experimental results show the policy achieves low stockout (2.9%) and inventory-full (1.1%) probabilities over a 200-step horizon, primarily relying on inventory age distribution, with counterfactual analysis indicating medium-large orders are placed in well-buffered states without compromising safety.
本研究旨在解决安全关键型医疗供应链中决策需可信与透明的问题，应用COOL-MC工具对血小板库存管理的强化学习策略进行验证和解释，以平衡过期浪费和短缺风险。方法结合强化学习、概率模型检验和可解释人工智能，通过构建策略诱导的马尔可夫链来验证概率计算树逻辑属性并提供特征级解释。实验结果表明，该策略在200步范围内实现了较低的缺货概率（2.9%）和库存满载概率（1.1%），主要关注库存年龄分布而非其他特征，反事实分析显示中等偏大订单在缓冲充足状态下发出且几乎不影响安全概率。
Skywork-Reward-V2: Scaling Preference Data Curation via Human-AI Synergy
Authors: Chris Yuhao Liu, Liang Zeng, Yuzhen Xiao, Jujie He, Jiacai Liu, Chaojie Wang, Rui Yan, Wei Shen, Fuxiang Zhang, Jiacheng Xu, Yang Liu, Yahui Zhou
Venue: ICLR 2026 Poster
First: 2025-07-02T04:40:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T20:56:17+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026 Poster
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the critical role of reward models (RMs) in Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF), current state-of-the-art open RMs perform poorly on most existing evaluation benchmarks, failing to capture nuanced human preferences. We hypothesize that this brittleness stems primarily from limitations in preference datasets, which are often narrowly scoped, synthetically labeled, or lack rigorous quality control. To address these challenges, we present SynPref-40M, a large-scale preference dataset comprising 40 million preference pairs. To enable data curation at scale, we design a human-AI synergistic two-stage pipeline that leverages the complementary strengths of human annotation quality and AI scalability. In this pipeline, humans provide verified annotations, while LLMs perform automatic curation based on human guidance. Training on this preference mixture, we introduce Skywork-Reward-V2, a suite of eight reward models ranging from 0.6B to 8B parameters, trained on a carefully curated subset of 26 million preference pairs from SynPref-40M. We demonstrate that Skywork-Reward-V2 is versatile across a wide range of capabilities, including alignment with human preferences, objective correctness, safety, resistance to stylistic biases, and best-of-N scaling. These reward models achieve state-of-the-art performance across seven major reward model benchmarks, outperform generative reward models, and demonstrate strong downstream performance. Ablation studies confirm that effectiveness stems not only from data scale but also from high-quality curation. The Skywork-Reward-V2 series represents substantial progress in open reward models, demonstrating how human-AI curation synergy can unlock significantly higher data quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Skywork-Reward-V2：通过人机协同扩展偏好数据精炼
尽管奖励模型在基于人类反馈的强化学习中具有关键作用，但当前最先进的开放奖励模型在多数现有评估基准上表现不佳，难以捕捉细微的人类偏好。我们认为这种脆弱性主要源于偏好数据集的局限性——这些数据集往往范围狭窄、采用合成标注或缺乏严格的质量控制。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了SynPref-40M，这是一个包含4000万偏好对的大规模偏好数据集。为实现规模化数据精炼，我们设计了一个人机协同的两阶段流程，充分利用人类标注质量与AI可扩展性的互补优势。在该流程中，人类提供经过验证的标注，而大语言模型则基于人类指导进行自动精炼。基于此混合偏好数据训练，我们推出了Skywork-Reward-V2系列——包含八个参数量从0.6B到8B的奖励模型，其训练数据来自SynPref-40M中经过精心筛选的2600万偏好对子集。实验表明，Skywork-Reward-V2在广泛能力维度上均表现优异，包括人类偏好对齐、客观正确性、安全性、风格偏见抵抗以及N选优扩展性。该系列模型在七大主流奖励模型基准测试中均达到最先进水平，超越生成式奖励模型，并展现出强大的下游任务性能。消融研究证实，其有效性不仅源于数据规模，更得益于高质量的数据精炼。Skywork-Reward-V2系列标志着开放奖励模型领域的重大进展，展示了人机协同精炼如何显著提升数据质量。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the poor performance of existing open reward models (RMs) in capturing nuanced human preferences, which is attributed to limitations in narrow, synthetic, or low-quality preference datasets, this paper introduces a human-AI synergistic two-stage pipeline to curate large-scale, high-quality data. The method involves humans providing verified annotations and LLMs performing automatic curation based on human guidance, resulting in SynPref-40M, a dataset of 40 million preference pairs, from which a subset of 26 million pairs is used to train Skywork-Reward-V2, a suite of eight RMs ranging from 0.6B to 8B parameters. Experimental results show that these models achieve state-of-the-art performance across seven major RM benchmarks, demonstrating versatility in alignment, correctness, safety, bias resistance, and scaling, with ablations confirming the importance of both data scale and curation quality.
针对现有开源奖励模型在捕捉人类细微偏好上表现不佳的问题，该研究认为这源于偏好数据集范围狭窄、合成标注或缺乏严格质量控制，因此提出了一种人机协同的两阶段流程来大规模构建高质量数据。该方法结合人类验证标注与基于人类指导的大语言模型自动筛选，创建了包含4000万偏好对的SynPref-40M数据集，并从中精选2600万对训练了Skywork-Reward-V2系列奖励模型，包含0.6B至8B参数的八个模型。实验结果表明，这些模型在七个主要奖励模型基准测试中达到最先进性能，在人类偏好对齐、客观正确性、安全性、风格偏见抵抗和最佳N选择扩展方面表现优异，消融研究证实了数据规模与高质量筛选的双重有效性。
A Reinforcement Learning Approach in Multi-Phase Second-Price Auction Design
Authors: Rui Ai, Boxiang Lyu, Zhaoran Wang, Zhuoran Yang, Michael I. Jordan
First: 2022-10-19T03:49:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T19:47:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study reserve price optimization in multi-phase second price auctions, where the seller's prior actions affect the bidders' later valuations through a Markov Decision Process (MDP). Compared to the bandit setting in existing works, the setting in ours involves three challenges. First, from the seller's perspective, we need to efficiently explore the environment in the presence of potentially untruthful bidders who aim to manipulate the seller's policy. Second, we want to minimize the seller's revenue regret when the market noise distribution is unknown. Third, the seller's per-step revenue is an unknown, nonlinear random variable, and cannot even be directly observed from the environment but realized values. We propose a mechanism addressing all three challenges. To address the first challenge, we use a combination of a new technique named "buffer periods" and inspirations from Reinforcement Learning (RL) with low switching cost to limit bidders' surplus from untruthful bidding, thereby incentivizing approximately truthful bidding. The second one is tackled by a novel algorithm that removes the need for pure exploration when the market noise distribution is unknown. The third challenge is resolved by an extension of LSVI-UCB, where we use the auction's underlying structure to control the uncertainty of the revenue function. The three techniques culminate in the Contextual-LSVI-UCB-Buffer (CLUB) algorithm which achieves $\tilde{O}(H^{5/2}\sqrt{K})$ revenue regret, where $K$ is the number of episodes and $H$ is the length of each episode, when the market noise is known and $\tilde{O}(H^{3}\sqrt{K})$ revenue regret when the noise is unknown with no assumptions on bidders' truthfulness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多阶段次价拍卖设计的强化学习方法
本研究探讨多阶段次价拍卖中的保留价优化问题，其中卖方前期行为通过马尔可夫决策过程影响竞拍者后续估值。相较于现有研究中的多臂赌博机设定，本文面临三重挑战：首先，在存在试图操纵卖方策略的非诚实竞拍者时，卖方需实现高效环境探索；其次，在市场噪声分布未知时最小化卖方收益遗憾；第三，卖方单步收益为不可直接观测的非线性随机变量。我们提出一种同时解决这三重挑战的机制：针对第一项挑战，结合'缓冲期'新技术与低切换成本的强化学习思想，限制非诚实竞价的竞拍者剩余；针对第二项挑战，提出无需纯探索阶段的新算法；针对第三项挑战，扩展LSVI-UCB算法并利用拍卖底层结构控制收益函数不确定性。最终形成的情境化LSVI-UCB-缓冲算法，在已知市场噪声时实现$\tilde{O}(H^{5/2}\sqrt{K})$收益遗憾，在噪声未知且不假设竞拍者诚实性时实现$\tilde{O}(H^{3}\sqrt{K})$收益遗憾，其中$K$为回合数，$H$为回合长度。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of optimizing reserve prices in multi-phase second-price auctions where bidders' valuations evolve via a Markov Decision Process, and bidders may act untruthfully to manipulate the seller. The proposed method, the Contextual-LSVI-UCB-Buffer (CLUB) algorithm, combines buffer periods to incentivize truthful bidding, a novel approach to eliminate pure exploration under unknown market noise, and an extension of LSVI-UCB to handle the unobserved, nonlinear revenue function. Experimental results show the algorithm achieves a revenue regret of Õ(H^{5/2}√K) with known market noise and Õ(H^{3}√K) with unknown noise, without requiring assumptions on bidder truthfulness.
本文研究了多阶段次价拍卖中的保留价优化问题，其中投标人的估值通过马尔可夫决策过程演化，且投标人可能采取不诚实行为以操纵卖家。所提出的方法，即上下文-LSVI-UCB-缓冲（CLUB）算法，结合了缓冲期以激励诚实投标、一种在未知市场噪声下消除纯探索的新方法，以及LSVI-UCB的扩展来处理未观测的非线性收益函数。实验结果表明，该算法在已知市场噪声时实现了Õ(H^{5/2}√K)的收益遗憾，在未知噪声时实现了Õ(H^{3}√K)的收益遗憾，且无需假设投标人的诚实性。
Distributional value gradients for stochastic environments
Authors: Baptiste Debes, Tinne Tuytelaars
First: 2026-01-27T21:31:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T19:16:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Gradient-regularized value learning methods improve sample efficiency by leveraging learned models of transition dynamics and rewards to estimate return gradients. However, existing approaches, such as MAGE, struggle in stochastic or noisy environments, limiting their applicability. In this work, we address these limitations by extending distributional reinforcement learning on continuous state-action spaces to model not only the distribution over scalar state-action value functions but also over their gradients. We refer to this approach as Distributional Sobolev Training. Inspired by Stochastic Value Gradients (SVG), our method utilizes a one-step world model of reward and transition distributions implemented via a conditional Variational Autoencoder (cVAE). The proposed framework is sample-based and employs Max-sliced Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MSMMD) to instantiate the distributional Bellman operator. We prove that the Sobolev-augmented Bellman operator is a contraction with a unique fixed point, and highlight a fundamental smoothness trade-off underlying contraction in gradient-aware RL. To validate our method, we first showcase its effectiveness on a simple stochastic reinforcement learning toy problem, then benchmark its performance on several MuJoCo environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：随机环境中的分布值梯度方法
梯度正则化价值学习方法通过利用习得的转移动态与奖励模型估计回报梯度，从而提升样本效率。然而，现有方法（如MAGE）在随机或噪声环境中表现欠佳，限制了其适用性。本研究通过将连续状态-动作空间的分布强化学习扩展至不仅建模标量状态-动作价值函数的分布，还建模其梯度分布，以解决上述局限。该方法被称为分布索伯列夫训练。受随机价值梯度（SVG）启发，本方法采用基于条件变分自编码器（cVAE）实现的奖励与转移分布单步世界模型。所提框架基于样本驱动，并采用最大切片最大均值差异（MSMMD）实例化分布贝尔曼算子。我们证明索伯列夫增强贝尔曼算子具有压缩性与唯一不动点，并揭示了梯度感知强化学习中压缩性背后的基本平滑度权衡。为验证方法有效性，我们首先在简单随机强化学习示例问题中展示其优势，随后在多个MuJoCo环境中进行性能基准测试。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing gradient-regularized value learning methods like MAGE, which perform poorly in stochastic environments, this paper introduces Distributional Sobolev Training to improve sample efficiency. The method extends distributional reinforcement learning to continuous spaces by modeling distributions over both state-action value functions and their gradients, using a one-step world model with a conditional VAE and a sample-based framework instantiated via Max-sliced Maximum Mean Discrepancy. Experimental results demonstrate the approach's effectiveness on a stochastic toy problem and show improved performance benchmarks on several MuJoCo environments, supported by theoretical proofs that the Sobolev-augmented Bellman operator is a contraction with a unique fixed point.
本文的动机是现有梯度正则化价值学习方法（如MAGE）在随机环境中表现不佳，限制了其适用性。为此，研究提出了分布索伯列夫训练方法，通过将分布强化学习扩展到连续状态-动作空间，不仅建模标量状态-动作价值函数的分布，还建模其梯度的分布。该方法采用条件变分自编码器实现的一步世界模型，并基于最大切片最大均值差异实例化分布贝尔曼算子。实验结果表明，该方法在一个简单的随机强化学习玩具问题上有效，并在多个MuJoCo环境中取得了性能提升，理论分析证明了索伯列夫增强贝尔曼算子是具有唯一不动点的压缩映射。
Estimate Hitting Time by Hitting Probability for Elitist Evolutionary Algorithms
Authors: Jun He, Siang Yew Chong, Xin Yao
Venue: IEEE Transactions on Evolutionary Computation 12 November 2025
First: 2025-06-18T16:25:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T19:10:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Drift analysis is a powerful tool for analyzing the time complexity of evolutionary algorithms. However, it requires manual construction of drift functions to bound hitting time for each specific algorithm and problem. To address this limitation, general linear drift functions were introduced for elitist evolutionary algorithms. But calculating linear bound coefficients effectively remains a problem. This paper proposes a new method called drift analysis of hitting probability to compute these coefficients. Each coefficient is interpreted as a bound on the hitting probability of a fitness level, transforming the task of estimating hitting time into estimating hitting probability. A novel drift analysis method is then developed to estimate hitting probability, where paths are introduced to handle multimodal fitness landscapes. Explicit expressions are constructed to compute hitting probability, significantly simplifying the estimation process. One advantage of the proposed method is its ability to estimate both the lower and upper bounds of hitting time and to compare the performance of two algorithms in terms of hitting time. To demonstrate this application, two algorithms for the knapsack problem, each incorporating feasibility rules and greedy repair respectively, are compared. The analysis indicates that neither constraint handling technique consistently outperforms the other.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于击中概率估计精英进化算法的击中时间
漂移分析是分析进化算法时间复杂度的有力工具，但需为每个具体算法和问题手动构建漂移函数以界定击中时间。为克服此局限，研究者为精英进化算法引入了通用线性漂移函数，但如何有效计算线性界系数仍是难题。本文提出一种称为击中概率漂移分析的新方法，将每个系数解释为适应度层级击中概率的界，从而将估计击中时间的任务转化为估计击中概率。通过引入路径处理多峰适应度地形，开发了新的漂移分析方法来估计击中概率，并构建显式表达式进行计算，大幅简化了估计流程。该方法的优势在于能同时估计击中时间的上下界，并比较两种算法在击中时间上的性能。为展示此应用，本文比较了背包问题的两种算法：分别采用可行性规则与贪心修复策略。分析表明，两种约束处理技术均未表现出持续优势。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge in drift analysis of manually constructing drift functions to bound hitting times for elitist evolutionary algorithms by proposing a new method that interprets drift coefficients as bounds on hitting probabilities, thereby transforming hitting time estimation into hitting probability estimation. The method introduces paths to handle multimodal fitness landscapes and constructs explicit expressions to compute hitting probabilities, simplifying the process and enabling estimation of both lower and upper bounds on hitting time as well as performance comparisons between algorithms. Experimental application to two knapsack problem algorithms with different constraint handling techniques shows that neither technique consistently outperforms the other, demonstrating the method's utility in comparative analysis.
本文针对精英进化算法的漂移分析中需手动构建漂移函数以界定命中时间的难题，提出了一种新方法，将漂移系数解释为命中概率的界限，从而将命中时间估计转化为命中概率估计。该方法引入路径处理多模态适应度地形，并构建显式表达式计算命中概率，简化了估计过程，能够同时估计命中时间的上下界并比较算法性能。通过对两种分别采用可行性规则和贪婪修复的背包问题算法进行实验比较，分析表明两种约束处理技术均未持续优于对方，验证了该方法在性能对比中的实用性。
Tool Verification for Test-Time Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ruotong Liao, Nikolai Röhrich, Xiaohan Wang, Yuhui Zhang, Yasaman Samadzadeh, Volker Tresp, Serena Yeung-Levy
First: 2026-03-02T18:57:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:57:52+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 11 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL) has emerged as a promising paradigm for self-evolving large reasoning models (LRMs), enabling online adaptation on unlabeled test inputs via self-induced rewards through majority voting. However, a spurious yet high-frequency unverified consensus can become a biased and reinforced reward signal, leading to incorrect mode collapse. We address this failure mode with T^3RL (Tool-Verification for Test-Time Reinforcement Learning), which introduces test-time tool verification into reward estimation. Concretely, a verifier uses an external tool as evidence (e.g., from code execution) to upweight verified rollouts in a verification-aware voting, producing more reliable pseudo-labels for training. Across various math difficulties (MATH-500, AMC, and AIME 2024) and diverse backbone types, T^3RL significantly improves over TTRL, with larger gains on harder problems. More broadly, T^3RL can be viewed as verified online data synthesis, highlighting test-time tool verification as a key mechanism for stabilizing self-evolution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：测试时强化学习的工具验证方法
测试时强化学习（TTRL）已成为自演进大型推理模型（LRMs）的重要范式，通过多数投票机制在无标注测试输入上实现基于自生成奖励的在线适应。然而，高频但未经核验的虚假共识可能形成有偏且被强化的奖励信号，导致错误的模式坍缩。我们提出T^3RL（测试时强化学习的工具验证方法），将测试时工具验证引入奖励估计过程。具体而言，验证器利用外部工具（如代码执行结果）作为证据，在验证感知的投票中提升已验证轨迹的权重，从而为训练生成更可靠的伪标签。在多种数学难度数据集（MATH-500、AMC及AIME 2024）和不同骨干模型上的实验表明，T^3RL较TTRL有显著提升，且在难题上增益更大。更广泛而言，T^3RL可视为经过验证的在线数据合成方法，凸显了测试时工具验证作为稳定自演进机制的关键作用。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the problem in test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL) where unverified majority voting can produce spurious, self-reinforcing reward signals leading to incorrect model behavior. To address this, the authors propose T^3RL, a method that integrates test-time tool verification, using external tools like code execution to provide evidence for verifying and upweighting reliable model rollouts during reward estimation. Experimental results across various math benchmarks (MATH-500, AMC, AIME 2024) and backbone models show that T^3RL significantly outperforms standard TTRL, with particularly strong improvements on harder problems, demonstrating its effectiveness as a mechanism for stabilizing online self-evolution.
本文的动机源于测试时强化学习中，未经验证的多数投票可能产生虚假且自我强化的奖励信号，导致模型行为错误。为解决这一问题，作者提出了T^3RL方法，该方法在奖励估计中引入了测试时工具验证，利用外部工具（如代码执行）作为证据来验证并加权可靠的模型推演。在多种数学基准（MATH-500、AMC、AIME 2024）和不同骨干模型上的实验结果表明，T^3RL显著优于标准测试时强化学习，尤其在难题上提升更大，证明了其作为稳定在线自我进化机制的有效性。
Return Augmented Decision Transformer for Off-Dynamics Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ruhan Wang, Yu Yang, Zhishuai Liu, Dongruo Zhou, Pan Xu
Venue: Transactions on Machine Learning Research, 2026
First: 2024-10-30T20:46:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:38:36+00:00
Comments: 26 pages, 11 tables, 8 figures. Published in Transactions on Machine Learning Research (TMLR)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study offline off-dynamics reinforcement learning (RL) to utilize data from an easily accessible source domain to enhance policy learning in a target domain with limited data. Our approach centers on return-conditioned supervised learning (RCSL), particularly focusing on Decision Transformer (DT) type frameworks, which can predict actions conditioned on desired return guidance and complete trajectory history. Previous works address the dynamics shift problem by augmenting the reward in the trajectory from the source domain to match the optimal trajectory in the target domain. However, this strategy can not be directly applicable in RCSL owing to (1) the unique form of the RCSL policy class, which explicitly depends on the return, and (2) the absence of a straightforward representation of the optimal trajectory distribution. We propose the Return Augmented (REAG) method for DT type frameworks, where we augment the return in the source domain by aligning its distribution with that in the target domain. We provide the theoretical analysis demonstrating that the RCSL policy learned from REAG achieves the same level of suboptimality as would be obtained without a dynamics shift. We introduce two practical implementations REAG$_\text{Dara}^{*}$ and REAG$_\text{MV}^{*}$ respectively. Thorough experiments on D4RL datasets and various DT-type baselines demonstrate that our methods consistently enhance the performance of DT type frameworks in off-dynamics RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向异动态强化学习的回报增强决策变换器
本研究针对离线异动态强化学习（RL），利用易获取的源域数据提升目标域（数据有限）的策略学习。方法核心是基于回报条件的监督学习（RCSL），聚焦于决策变换器（DT）类框架——该框架能根据期望回报指导和完整轨迹历史预测动作。先前研究通过调整源域轨迹的奖励以匹配目标域最优轨迹来解决动态偏移问题，但该策略无法直接适用于RCSL，原因在于：（1）RCSL策略类显式依赖回报的独特形式；（2）缺乏最优轨迹分布的直观表示。我们提出适用于DT类框架的回报增强（REAG）方法，通过对齐源域与目标域的回报分布实现源域回报增强。理论分析表明，基于REAG学习的RCSL策略能达到与无动态偏移时相当的次优性水平。我们进一步提出两种实践实现：REAG$_\text{Dara}^{*}$ 与 REAG$_\text{MV}^{*}$。在D4RL数据集及多种DT类基线模型上的系统实验表明，本方法能持续提升DT类框架在异动态RL中的性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses offline off-dynamics reinforcement learning, aiming to leverage abundant data from a source domain to improve policy learning in a target domain with scarce data, focusing on return-conditioned supervised learning frameworks like Decision Transformer. The proposed method, Return Augmented (REAG), tackles the dynamics shift by augmenting the return in source-domain trajectories to align its distribution with that of the target domain, circumventing limitations of prior reward-augmentation strategies that are incompatible with the return-dependent policy class and lack optimal trajectory representations. Theoretically, REAG ensures the learned policy achieves suboptimality comparable to scenarios without dynamics shift, and two practical implementations, REAG_Dara* and REAG_MV*, are introduced. Experimental results on D4RL datasets across various Decision Transformer baselines consistently show that REAG enhances performance in off-dynamics settings.
本文研究离线异动态强化学习，旨在利用源领域丰富数据提升目标领域数据有限时的策略学习，重点关注基于回报条件监督学习的决策变换器框架。所提出的回报增强方法通过调整源领域轨迹的回报分布以与目标领域对齐，解决了先前奖励增强策略因策略类显式依赖回报且缺乏最优轨迹表示而无法直接应用的动态偏移问题。理论分析表明，该方法学习的策略能达到与无动态偏移时相当的次优性，并引入了REAG_Dara*和REAG_MV*两种实践实现。在D4RL数据集和多种决策变换器基线上的全面实验证明，该方法能持续提升异动态强化学习中决策变换器框架的性能。
Near-Optimal Regret for KL-Regularized Multi-Armed Bandits
Authors: Kaixuan Ji, Qingyue Zhao, Heyang Zhao, Qiwei Di, Quanquan Gu
First: 2026-03-02T18:17:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:17:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent studies have shown that reinforcement learning with KL-regularized objectives can enjoy faster rates of convergence or logarithmic regret, in contrast to the classical $\sqrt{T}$-type regret in the unregularized setting. However, the statistical efficiency of online learning with respect to KL-regularized objectives remains far from completely characterized, even when specialized to multi-armed bandits (MABs). We address this problem for MABs via a sharp analysis of KL-UCB using a novel peeling argument, which yields a $\tilde{O}(ηK\log^2T)$ upper bound: the first high-probability regret bound with linear dependence on $K$. Here, $T$ is the time horizon, $K$ is the number of arms, $η^{-1}$ is the regularization intensity, and $\tilde{O}$ hides all logarithmic factors except those involving $\log T$. The near-tightness of our analysis is certified by the first non-constant lower bound $Ω(ηK \log T)$, which follows from subtle hard-instance constructions and a tailored decomposition of the Bayes prior. Moreover, in the low-regularization regime (i.e., large $η$), we show that the KL-regularized regret for MABs is $η$-independent and scales as $\tildeΘ(\sqrt{KT})$. Overall, our results provide a thorough understanding of KL-regularized MABs across all regimes of $η$ and yield nearly optimal bounds in terms of $K$, $η$, and $T$.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KL正则化多臂老虎机的近最优遗憾界
近期研究表明，与经典无正则化设定中$\sqrt{T}$型遗憾相比，采用KL正则化目标的强化学习可获得更快的收敛速度或对数遗憾。然而，即使专门针对多臂老虎机问题，在线学习在KL正则化目标下的统计效率仍远未完全刻画。我们通过新颖的剥离论证对KL-UCB算法进行精细分析，首次得到具有线性$K$依赖性的高概率遗憾上界$\tilde{O}(ηK\log^2T)$，其中$T$为时间跨度，$K$为臂数，$η^{-1}$为正则化强度，$\tilde{O}$隐藏除$\log T$外的所有对数因子。通过精妙的困难实例构造和贝叶斯先验的定制分解，我们首次给出非恒定下界$Ω(ηK \log T)$，证明了分析的近紧性。此外，在低正则化区域（即$η$较大时），我们证明KL正则化遗憾与$η$无关且具有$\tildeΘ(\sqrt{KT})$量级。总体而言，我们的研究完整刻画了KL正则化多臂老虎机在所有$η$区域的行为，并在$K$、$η$、$T$维度上给出了近乎最优的边界。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the statistical efficiency of KL-regularized multi-armed bandits, motivated by the need to better characterize the convergence and regret properties of reinforcement learning with KL-regularized objectives, which have shown promise for faster convergence compared to unregularized settings. The method employs a sharp analysis of the KL-UCB algorithm using a novel peeling argument to derive high-probability regret bounds. The main experimental results establish a near-optimal upper bound of Õ(ηK log²T) and a matching lower bound of Ω(ηK log T), revealing a linear dependence on the number of arms K; additionally, in the low-regularization regime, the regret is shown to be η-independent and scales as Õ(√KT), providing a comprehensive understanding across all regularization intensities.
本文研究了KL正则化多臂老虎机的统计效率，其动机在于需要更好地刻画KL正则化目标在强化学习中的收敛和遗憾特性，这类目标相比无正则化设置已显示出更快的收敛潜力。方法上，通过对KL-UCB算法采用新颖的剥离论证进行精细分析，以推导高概率遗憾界。主要实验结果表明，该研究建立了近乎最优的遗憾上界Õ(ηK log²T)和下界Ω(ηK log T)，揭示了遗憾与臂数K的线性依赖关系；此外，在低正则化区域，遗憾被证明与η无关且按Õ(√KT)缩放，从而对所有正则化强度提供了全面理解。
Data-to-Energy Stochastic Dynamics
Authors: Kirill Tamogashev, Nikolay Malkin
First: 2025-09-30T15:03:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:11:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The Schrödinger bridge problem is concerned with finding a stochastic dynamical system bridging two marginal distributions that minimises a certain transportation cost. This problem, which represents a generalisation of optimal transport to the stochastic case, has received attention due to its connections to diffusion models and flow matching, as well as its applications in the natural sciences. However, all existing algorithms allow to infer such dynamics only for cases where samples from both distributions are available. In this paper, we propose the first general method for modelling Schrödinger bridges when one (or both) distributions are given by their unnormalised densities, with no access to data samples. Our algorithm relies on a generalisation of the iterative proportional fitting (IPF) procedure to the data-free case, inspired by recent developments in off-policy reinforcement learning for training of diffusion samplers. We demonstrate the efficacy of the proposed data-to-energy IPF on synthetic problems, finding that it can successfully learn transports between multimodal distributions. As a secondary consequence of our reinforcement learning formulation, which assumes a fixed time discretisation scheme for the dynamics, we find that existing data-to-data Schrödinger bridge algorithms can be substantially improved by learning the diffusion coefficient of the dynamics. Finally, we apply the newly developed algorithm to the problem of sampling posterior distributions in latent spaces of generative models, thus creating a data-free image-to-image translation method. Code: https://github.com/mmacosha/d2e-stochastic-dynamics
中文标题/摘要
标题：数据到能量的随机动力学
薛定谔桥问题旨在寻找连接两个边缘分布的随机动力系统，以最小化特定传输成本。该问题将最优传输推广至随机情形，因其与扩散模型、流匹配的联系及其在自然科学中的应用而备受关注。然而，现有算法仅适用于可从两个分布获取样本的情形。本文首次提出一种通用方法，用于在分布（一个或两个）仅通过未归一化密度函数给出、且无法获取数据样本时建模薛定谔桥。受近期扩散采样器训练的离策略强化学习进展启发，本算法将迭代比例拟合（IPF）过程推广至无数据场景。我们在合成问题上验证了所提数据到能量IPF的有效性，发现其能成功学习多峰分布间的传输。作为强化学习公式的次要成果（该公式假设动力学采用固定时间离散方案），我们发现通过学习动力学的扩散系数，可显著改进现有数据到数据薛定谔桥算法。最后，我们将新算法应用于生成模型隐空间中后验分布的采样问题，从而创建了一种无数据的图像到图像转换方法。代码：https://github.com/mmacosha/d2e-stochastic-dynamics
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation in existing Schrödinger bridge algorithms, which require samples from both distributions, by proposing a novel method that works when one or both distributions are specified only by their unnormalized densities without data samples. The method generalizes the iterative proportional fitting (IPF) procedure to this data-free setting, drawing inspiration from off-policy reinforcement learning techniques used in diffusion sampler training. Experimental results on synthetic problems show the method successfully learns transports between multimodal distributions, and an application to sampling posterior distributions in generative model latent spaces demonstrates its utility as a data-free image-to-image translation technique.

MuFlex: A Scalable, Physics-based Platform for Multi-Building Flexibility Analysis and Coordination
Authors: Ziyan Wu, Ivan Korolija, Rui Tang
First: 2025-08-19T05:44:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:55:58+00:00
Comments: The platform is released open-source on GitHub: https://github.com/BuildNexusX/MuFlex
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
With the increasing penetration of renewable generation on the power grid, maintaining system balance requires coordinated demand flexibility from aggregations of buildings. Reinforcement learning has been widely explored for building controls because of its model-free nature. Open-source simulation testbeds are essential not only for training RL agents but also for fairly benchmarking control strategies. However, most building-sector testbeds target single buildings; multi-building platforms are relatively limited and typically rely on simplified models (e.g., Resistance-Capacitance) or data-driven approaches, which lack the ability to fully capture the physical intricacies and intermediate variables necessary for interpreting control performance. Moreover, these platforms often impose fixed inputs, outputs, and model formats, restricting their applicability as benchmarking tools across diverse control scenarios. To address these gaps, MuFlex, a scalable, open-source platform for multi-building flexibility coordination, was developed. MuFlex enables synchronous information exchange and co-simulation across multiple detailed building models programmed in EnergyPlus and Modelica, and adheres to the latest OpenAI Gym interface, providing a modular, standardized RL implementation. The platform's physics-based capabilities and workflow were demonstrated in a case study coordinating demand flexibility across four office buildings using the Soft Actor-Critic algorithm. The results show that under four buildings' coordination, SAC effectively reduced the aggregated peak demand by nearly 12% with maintained indoor comfort to ensure the power demand below the threshold. Additionally, the platform's scalability was investigated through computational benchmarking on building clusters with varying sizes, model types, and simulation programs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MuFlex：基于物理模型的可扩展多建筑灵活性分析与协调平台

Motivated by the need for scalable testbeds to coordinate building demand flexibility for grid balance amid renewable integration, this paper introduces MuFlex, an open-source platform that enables synchronous co-simulation of multiple detailed physics-based building models (EnergyPlus/Modelica) via a standardized OpenAI Gym interface for reinforcement learning. The method employs a modular architecture to facilitate flexible benchmarking of control strategies, demonstrated in a case study where the Soft Actor-Critic algorithm coordinated four office buildings, reducing aggregated peak demand by nearly 12% while maintaining indoor comfort below a power threshold.
